 <p><a name="an_40:3">40:3</a> And he hath put a new song in my mouth, even praise to our God: many shall see it, and fear, and shall trust in the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:4">40:4</a> Blessed is that man that maketh the LORD his trust, and respecteth not the proud, nor such as turn aside to lies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:5">40:5</a> Many, O LORD, my God, are thy wonderful works which thou hast done, and thy thoughts which are toward us, they cannot be reckoned up in order to thee: if I would declare and speak of them, they are more than can be numbered. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:6">40:6</a> Sacrifice and offering thou didst not desire; my ears hast thou opened: burnt-offering and sin-offering hast thou not required. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:7">40:7</a> Then said I, Lo, I come: in the volume of the book it is written of me, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:8">40:8</a> I delight to do thy will, O my God: yea, thy law is within my heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:9">40:9</a> I have preached righteousness in the great congregation: lo, I have not refrained my lips, O LORD, thou knowest. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:10">40:10</a> I have not hid thy righteousness within my heart; I have declared thy faithfulness and thy salvation: I have not concealed thy loving-kindness and thy truth from the great congregation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:11">40:11</a> Withhold not thou thy tender mercies from me, O LORD: let thy loving-kindness and thy truth continually preserve me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:12">40:12</a> For innumerable evils have encompassed me: my iniquities have taken hold upon me, so that I am not able to look up; they are more than the hairs of my head: therefore my heart faileth me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:13">40:13</a> Be pleased, O LORD, to deliver me: O LORD, make haste to help me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:14">40:14</a> Let them be ashamed and confounded together that seek after my soul to destroy it; let them be driven backward and put to shame that wish me evil. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:15">40:15</a> Let them be desolate for a reward of their shame that say to me, Aha, aha. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:16">40:16</a> Let all those that seek thee rejoice and be glad in thee: let such as love thy salvation say continually, The LORD be magnified. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:17">40:17</a> But I am poor and needy; yet the Lord thinketh upon me: thou art my help and my deliverer; make no delay, O my God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:1">41:1</a> To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David. Blessed is he that considereth the poor: the LORD will deliver him in the time of trouble. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:2">41:2</a> The LORD will preserve him, and keep him alive; and he shall be blessed upon the earth: and thou wilt not deliver him to the will of his enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:3">41:3</a> The LORD will strengthen him upon the bed of languishing: thou wilt make all his bed in his sickness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:4">41:4</a> I said, LORD, be merciful to me: heal my soul; for I have sinned against thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:5">41:5</a> My enemies speak evil of me, When shall he die, and his name perish? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:6">41:6</a> And if he cometh to see me, he speaketh vanity: his heart gathereth iniquity to itself; when he goeth abroad, he telleth it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:7">41:7</a> All that hate me whisper together against me: against me do they devise my hurt. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:8">41:8</a> An evil disease, say they, cleaveth fast to him: and now that he lieth he shall rise no more. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:9">41:9</a> Yes, my own familiar friend, in whom I trusted, who ate of my bread, hath lifted up his heel against me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:10">41:10</a> But thou, O LORD, be merciful to me, and raise me up, that I may requite them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:11">41:11</a> By this I know that thou favorest me, because my enemy doth not triumph over me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:12">41:12</a> And as for me, thou upholdest me in my integrity, and settest me before thy face for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:13">41:13</a> Blessed be the LORD God of Israel from everlasting, and to everlasting. Amen, and amen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:1">42:1</a> To the chief Musician, Maschil, for the sons of Korah. As the hart panteth after the water brooks, so my soul panteth after thee, O God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:2">42:2</a> My soul thirsteth for God, for the living God: when shall I come and appear before God? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:3">42:3</a> My tears have been my food day and night, while they continually say to me, Where is thy God? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:4">42:4</a> When I remember these things, I pour out my soul in me: for I had gone with the multitude, I went with them to the house of God, with the voice of joy and praise, with a multitude that kept holy-day. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:5">42:5</a> Why art thou cast down, O my soul? and why art thou disquieted in me? hope thou in God: for I shall yet praise him for the help of his countenance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:6">42:6</a> O my God, my soul is cast down within me: therefore will I remember thee from the land of Jordan, and of the Hermonites, from the hill Mizar. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:7">42:7</a> Deep calleth to deep at the noise of thy water-spouts: all thy waves and thy billows are gone over me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:8">42:8</a> Yet the LORD will command his loving-kindness in the day-time, and in the night his song shall be with me, and my prayer to the God of my life. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:9">42:9</a> I will say to God my rock, Why hast thou forgotten me? why go I mourning because of the oppression of the enemy? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:10">42:10</a> As with a sword in my bones, my enemies reproach me; while they say daily to me, Where is thy God? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:11">42:11</a> Why art thou cast down, O my soul? and why art thou disquieted within me? hope thou in God: for I shall yet praise him, who is the health of my countenance, and my God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:1">43:1</a> Judge me, O God, and plead my cause against an ungodly nation: O deliver me from the deceitful and unjust man. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:2">43:2</a> For thou art the God of my strength: why dost thou cast me off? why go I mourning because of the oppression of the enemy? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:3">43:3</a> O send out thy light and thy truth: let them lead me; let them bring me to thy holy hill, and to thy tabernacles. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:4">43:4</a> Then will I go to the altar of God, to God, my exceeding joy: yes, upon the harp will I praise thee, O God my God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:5">43:5</a> Why art thou cast down, O my soul? and why art thou disquieted within me? hope in God: for I shall yet praise him, who is the health of my countenance, and my God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:1">44:1</a> To the chief Musician for the sons of Korah, Maschil. We have heard with our ears, O God, our fathers have told us, what work thou didst in their days, in the times of old. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:2">44:2</a> How thou didst drive out the heathen with thy hand, and didst plant them; how thou didst afflict the people, and cast them out. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:3">44:3</a> For they obtained not the land in possession by their own sword, neither did their own arm save them: but thy right hand, and thy arm, and the light of thy countenance, because thou hadst a favor to them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:4">44:4</a> Thou art my King, O God: command deliverances for Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:5">44:5</a> Through thee will we push down our enemies: through thy name we will tread them under that rise up against us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:6">44:6</a> For I will not trust in my bow, neither shall my sword save me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:7">44:7</a> But thou hast saved us from our enemies, and hast put them to shame that hated us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:8">44:8</a> In God we boast all the day long, and praise thy name for ever. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:9">44:9</a> But thou hast cast off, and put us to shame; and goest not forth with our armies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:10">44:10</a> Thou makest us to turn back from the enemy: and they who hate us plunder for themselves. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:11">44:11</a> Thou hast given us like sheep appointed for food; and hast scattered us among the heathen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:12">44:12</a> Thou sellest thy people for naught, and dost not increase thy wealth by their price. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:13">44:13</a> Thou makest us a reproach to our neighbors, a scorn and a derision to them that are around us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:14">44:14</a> Thou makest us a by-word among the heathen, a shaking of the head among the people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:15">44:15</a> My confusion is continually before me, and the shame of my face hath covered me, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:16">44:16</a> For the voice of him that reproacheth and blasphemeth; by reason of the enemy and avenger. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:17">44:17</a> All this is come upon us; yet we have not forgotten thee, neither have we dealt falsely in thy covenant. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:18">44:18</a> Our heart is not turned back, neither have our steps declined from thy way; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:19">44:19</a> Though thou hast severely broke us in the place of dragons, and covered us with the shades of death. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:20">44:20</a> If we have forgotten the name of our God, or stretched out our hands to a strange god; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:21">44:21</a> Will not God search out this? for he knoweth the secrets of the heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:22">44:22</a> Yes, for thy sake are we killed all the day long; we are counted as sheep for the slaughter. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:23">44:23</a> Awake, why sleepest thou, O Lord? arise, cast us not off for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:24">44:24</a> Why hidest thou thy face, and forgettest our affliction and our oppression? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:25">44:25</a> For our soul is bowed down to the dust: our belly cleaveth to the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:26">44:26</a> Arise for our help, and redeem us for thy mercies' sake. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:1">45:1</a> To the chief Musician upon Shoshannim, for the sons of Korah, Maschil, A Song of loves. My heart is inditing a good matter: I speak of the things which I have made concerning the king: my tongue is the pen of a ready writer. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:2">45:2</a> Thou art fairer than the children of men: grace is poured into thy lips: therefore God hath blessed thee for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:3">45:3</a> Gird thy sword upon thy thigh, O most mighty, with thy glory and thy majesty. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:4">45:4</a> And in thy majesty ride prosperously because of truth and meekness and righteousness; and thy right hand shall teach thee terrible things. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:5">45:5</a> Thy arrows are sharp in the heart of the king's enemies; by which the people fall under thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:6">45:6</a> Thy throne, O God, is for ever and ever: the scepter of thy kingdom is a scepter of justice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:7">45:7</a> Thou lovest righteousness, and hatest wickedness: therefore God, thy God, hath anointed thee with the oil of gladness above thy fellows. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:8">45:8</a> All thy garments smell of myrrh, and aloes, and cassia, out of the ivory palaces, by which they have made thee glad. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:9">45:9</a> Kings daughters were among thy honorable women: upon thy right hand stood the queen in gold of Ophir. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:10">45:10</a> Hearken, O daughter, and consider, and incline thy ear; forget also thy own people, and thy father's house; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:11">45:11</a> So shall the king greatly desire thy beauty: for he is thy lord; and worship thou him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:12">45:12</a> And the daughter of Tyre shall be there with a gift; even the rich among the people shall entreat thy favor. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:13">45:13</a> The king's daughter is all glorious within: her clothing is of wrought gold. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:14">45:14</a> She shall be brought to the king in raiment of needle-work: the virgins her companions that follow her shall be brought to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:15">45:15</a> With gladness and rejoicing shall they be brought: they shall enter into the king's palace. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:16">45:16</a> Instead of thy fathers shall be thy children, whom thou mayest make princes in all the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:17">45:17</a> I will make thy name to be remembered in all generations: therefore shall the people praise thee for ever and ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:1">46:1</a> To the chief Musician for the sons of Korah, A Song upon Alamoth. God is our refuge and strength, a very present help in trouble. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:2">46:2</a> Therefore will we not fear, though the earth shall be removed, and though the mountains shall be carried into the midst of the sea; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:3">46:3</a> Though its waters shall roar and be disturbed, though the mountains shake with the swelling of it. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:4">46:4</a> There is a river, the streams of which shall make glad the city of God, the holy place of the tabernacles of the Most High. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:5">46:5</a> God is in the midst of her; she shall not be moved: God shall help her, and that right early. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:6">46:6</a> The heathen raged, the kingdoms were moved: he uttered his voice, the earth melted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:7">46:7</a> The LORD of hosts is with us; the God of Jacob is our refuge. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:8">46:8</a> Come, behold the works of the LORD, what desolations he hath made in the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:9">46:9</a> He maketh wars to cease to the end of the earth; he breaketh the bow, and cutteth the spear asunder; he burneth the chariot in the fire. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:10">46:10</a> Be still, and know that I am God: I will be exalted among the heathen, I will be exalted in the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:11">46:11</a> The LORD of hosts is with us; the God of Jacob is our refuge. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:1">47:1</a> To the chief Musician, A Psalm for the sons of Korah. O clap your hands, all ye people; shout to God with the voice of triumph. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:2">47:2</a> For the LORD most high is terrible; he is a great King over all the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:3">47:3</a> He shall subdue the people under us, and the nations under our feet. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:4">47:4</a> He shall choose our inheritance for us, the excellence of Jacob whom he loved. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:5">47:5</a> God is gone up with a shout, the LORD with the sound of a trumpet. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:6">47:6</a> Sing praises to God, sing praises: sing praises to our King, sing praises. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:7">47:7</a> For God is the King of all the earth: sing ye praises with understanding. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:8">47:8</a> God reigneth over the heathen: God sitteth upon the throne of his holiness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:9">47:9</a> The princes of the people are assembled, even the people of the God of Abraham: for the shields of the earth belong to God: he is greatly exalted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:1">48:1</a> A Song and Psalm for the sons of Korah. Great is the LORD, and greatly to be praised in the city of our God, in the mountain of his holiness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:2">48:2</a> Beautiful for situation, the joy of the whole earth, is mount Zion, on the sides of the north, the city of the great King. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:3">48:3</a> God is known in her palaces for a refuge. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:4">48:4</a> For lo, the kings were assembled, they passed by together. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:5">48:5</a> They saw it, and so they wondered; they were troubled, and hasted away. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:6">48:6</a> Fear took hold upon them there, and pain, as of a woman in travail. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:7">48:7</a> Thou breakest the ships of Tarshish with an east wind. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:8">48:8</a> As we have heard, so have we seen in the city of the LORD of hosts, in the city of our God: God will establish it for ever. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:9">48:9</a> We have thought of thy loving-kindness, O God, in the midst of thy temple. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:10">48:10</a> According to thy name, O God, so is thy praise to the ends of the earth: thy right hand is full of righteousness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:11">48:11</a> Let mount Zion rejoice, let the daughters of Judah be glad, because of thy judgments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:12">48:12</a> Walk about Zion, and go round her: number her towers. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:13">48:13</a> Mark ye well her bulwarks, consider her palaces; that ye may tell it to the generation following. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:14">48:14</a> For this God is our God for ever and ever: he will be our guide even to death. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:1">49:1</a> To the chief Musician, A Psalm for the sons of Korah. Hear this, all ye people; give ear, all ye inhabitants of the world: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:2">49:2</a> Both low and high, rich and poor together. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:3">49:3</a> My mouth shall speak of wisdom; and the meditation of my heart shall be of understanding. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:4">49:4</a> I will incline my ear to a parable: I will open my dark saying upon the harp. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:5">49:5</a> Why should I fear in the days of evil, when the iniquity of my heels shall encompass me? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:6">49:6</a> They that trust in their wealth, and boast themselves in the multitude of their riches; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:7">49:7</a> None of them can by any means redeem his brother, nor give to God a ransom for him: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:8">49:8</a> (For the redemption of their soul is precious, and it ceaseth for ever:) </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:9">49:9</a> That he should still live for ever, and not see corruption. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:10">49:10</a> For he seeth that wise men die, likewise the fool and the brutish person perish, and leave their wealth to others. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:11">49:11</a> Their inward thought is, that their houses shall continue for ever, and their dwelling places to all generations; they call their lands after their own names. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:12">49:12</a> Nevertheless man being in honor abideth not: he is like the beasts that perish. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:13">49:13</a> This their way is their folly: yet their posterity approve their sayings. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:14">49:14</a> Like sheep they are laid in the grave; death shall feed on them; and the upright shall have dominion over them in the morning; and their beauty shall consume in the grave from their dwelling. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:15">49:15</a> But God will redeem my soul from the power of the grave: for he shall receive me. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:16">49:16</a> Be not thou afraid when one is made rich, when the glory of his house is increased; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:17">49:17</a> For when he dieth he shall carry nothing away: his glory shall not descend after him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:18">49:18</a> Though while he lived he blessed his soul: and men will praise thee, when thou doest well to thyself. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:19">49:19</a> He shall go to the generation of his fathers; they shall never see light. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:20">49:20</a> Man that is in honor, and understandeth not, is like the beasts that perish. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:1">50:1</a> A Psalm of Asaph. The mighty God, even the LORD, hath spoken, and called the earth from the rising to the setting of the sun. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:2">50:2</a> Out of Zion, the perfection of beauty, God hath shined. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:3">50:3</a> Our God shall come, and shall not keep silence: a fire shall devour before him, and it shall be very tempestuous around him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:4">50:4</a> He shall call to the heavens from above, and to the earth, that he may judge his people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:5">50:5</a> Gather my saints together to me; those that have made a covenant with me by sacrifice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:6">50:6</a> And the heavens shall declare his righteousness: for God is judge himself. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:7">50:7</a> Hear, O my people, and I will speak; O Israel, and I will testify against thee: I am God, even thy God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:8">50:8</a> I will not reprove thee for thy sacrifices or thy burnt-offerings, to have been continually before me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:9">50:9</a> I will take no bullock out of thy house, nor he-goats out of thy folds. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:10">50:10</a> For every beast of the forest is mine, and the cattle upon a thousand hills. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:11">50:11</a> I know all the fowls of the mountains: and the wild beasts of the field are mine. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:12">50:12</a> If I were hungry, I would not tell thee: for the world is mine, and the fullness thereof. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:13">50:13</a> Will I eat the flesh of bulls, or drink the blood of goats? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:14">50:14</a> Offer to God thanksgiving; and pay thy vows to the Most High: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:15">50:15</a> And call upon me in the day of trouble: I will deliver thee, and thou shalt glorify me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:16">50:16</a> But to the wicked God saith, What hast thou to do to declare my statutes, or that thou shouldest take my covenant in thy mouth? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:17">50:17</a> Seeing thou hatest instruction, and castest my words behind thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:18">50:18</a> When thou sawest a thief, then thou consentedst with him, and hast been partaker with adulterers. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:19">50:19</a> Thou givest thy mouth to evil, and thy tongue frameth deceit. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:20">50:20</a> Thou sittest and speakest against thy brother; thou slanderest thy own mother's son. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:21">50:21</a> These things hast thou done, and I kept silence; thou thoughtest that I was altogether such an one as thyself: but I will reprove thee, and set them in order before thine eyes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:22">50:22</a> Now consider this, ye that forget God, lest I tear you in pieces, and there be none to deliver. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:23">50:23</a> Whoever offereth praise glorifieth me: and to him that ordereth his deportment aright will I show the salvation of God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:1">51:1</a> To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David, when Nathan the prophet came to him, after he had gone in to Bath-sheba. Have mercy upon me, O God, according to thy loving-kindness: according to the multitude of thy tender mercies, blot out my transgressions. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:2">51:2</a> Wash me thoroughly from my iniquity, and cleanse me from my sin. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:3">51:3</a> For I acknowledge my transgressions: and my sin is ever before me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:4">51:4</a> Against thee, thee only, have I sinned, and done this evil in thy sight: that thou mayest be justified when thou speakest, and be clear when thou judgest. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:5">51:5</a> Behold, I was shapen in iniquity; and in sin did my mother conceive me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:6">51:6</a> Behold, thou desirest truth in the inward parts: and in the hidden part thou shalt make me to know wisdom. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:7">51:7</a> Purge me with hyssop, and I shall be clean: wash me, and I shall be whiter than snow. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:8">51:8</a> Make me to hear joy and gladness; that the bones which thou hast broken may rejoice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:9">51:9</a> Hide thy face from my sins, and blot out all my iniquities. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:10">51:10</a> Create in me a clean heart, O God; and renew a right spirit within me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:11">51:11</a> Cast me not away from thy presence; and take not thy holy spirit from me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:12">51:12</a> Restore to me the joy of thy salvation; and uphold me with thy free spirit. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:13">51:13</a> Then will I teach transgressors thy ways; and sinners shall be converted to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:14">51:14</a> Deliver me from blood-guiltiness, O God, thou God of my salvation: and my tongue shall sing aloud of thy righteousness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:15">51:15</a> O Lord, open thou my lips; and my mouth shall show forth thy praise. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:16">51:16</a> For thou desirest not sacrifice: else would I give it: thou delightest not in burnt-offering. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:17">51:17</a> The sacrifices of God are a broken spirit: a broken and a contrite heart, O God, thou wilt not despise. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:18">51:18</a> Do good in thy good pleasure to Zion: build thou the walls of Jerusalem. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:19">51:19</a> Then shalt thou be pleased with the sacrifices of righteousness, with burnt-offering and whole burnt-offering: then shall they offer bullocks upon thy altar. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:1">52:1</a> To the chief Musician, Maschil, A Psalm of David, when Doeg the Edomite came and told Saul, and said to him, David is come to the house of Ahimelech. Why boastest thou thyself in mischief, O mighty man? the goodness of God endureth continually. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:2">52:2</a> Thy tongue deviseth mischiefs; like a sharp razor, working deceitfully. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:3">52:3</a> Thou lovest evil more than good; and lying rather than to speak righteousness. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:4">52:4</a> Thou lovest all devouring words, O thou deceitful tongue. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:5">52:5</a> God shall likewise destroy thee for ever, he shall take thee away, and pluck thee out of thy dwelling-place, and root thee out of the land of the living. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:6">52:6</a> The righteous also shall see, and fear, and shall laugh at him: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:7">52:7</a> Lo, this is the man that made not God his strength; but trusted in the abundance of his riches, and strengthened himself in his wickedness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:8">52:8</a> But I am like a green olive tree in the house of God: I trust in the mercy of God for ever and ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:9">52:9</a> I will praise thee for ever, because thou hast done it: and I will wait on thy name; for it is good before thy saints. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:1">53:1</a> To the chief Musician upon Mahalath, Maschil, A Psalm of David. The fool hath said in his heart, There is no God. They are corrupt, and have done abominable iniquity: there is none that doeth good. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:2">53:2</a> God looked down from heaven upon the children of men, to see if there were any that did understand, that did seek God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:3">53:3</a> Every one of them is gone back: they are altogether become filthy; there is none that doeth good, no, not one. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:4">53:4</a> Have the workers of iniquity no knowledge? who eat up my people as they eat bread! they have not called upon God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:5">53:5</a> There they were in great fear, where no fear was: for God hath scattered the bones of him that encampeth against thee: thou hast put them to shame, because God hath despised them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:6">53:6</a> O that the salvation of Israel were come out of Zion! when God bringeth back the captivity of his people, Jacob shall rejoice, and Israel shall be glad. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:1">54:1</a> To the chief Musician on Neginoth, Maschil, A Psalm of David, when the Ziphims came and said to Saul, Doth not David hide himself with us? Save me, O God, by thy name, and judge me by thy strength. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:2">54:2</a> Hear my prayer, O God; give ear to the words of my mouth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:3">54:3</a> For strangers have risen up against me, and oppressors seek after my soul: they have not set God before them. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:4">54:4</a> Behold, God is my helper: the Lord is with them that uphold my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:5">54:5</a> He will reward evil to my enemies; cut them off in thy truth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:6">54:6</a> I will freely sacrifice to thee: I will praise thy name, O LORD; for it is good. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:7">54:7</a> For he hath delivered me out of all trouble: and my eye hath seen its desire upon my enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:1">55:1</a> To the chief Musician on Neginoth, Maschil, A Psalm of David. Give ear to my prayer, O God; and hide not thyself from my supplication. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:2">55:2</a> Attend to me, and hear me: I mourn in my complaint, and make a noise; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:3">55:3</a> Because of the voice of the enemy, because of the oppression of the wicked: for they cast iniquity upon me, and in wrath they hate me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:4">55:4</a> My heart is severely pained within me: and the terrors of death have fallen upon me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:5">55:5</a> Fearfulness and trembling have come upon me, and horror hath overwhelmed me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:6">55:6</a> And I said, O that I had wings like a dove! for then I would fly away, and be at rest. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:7">55:7</a> Lo, then I would wander far off, and remain in the wilderness. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:8">55:8</a> I would hasten my escape from the windy storm and tempest. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:9">55:9</a> Destroy, O Lord, and divide their tongues: for I have seen violence and strife in the city. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:10">55:10</a> Day and night they go about it upon its walls: mischief also and sorrow are in the midst of it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:11">55:11</a> Wickedness is in the midst of it: deceit and guile depart not from her streets. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:12">55:12</a> For it was not an enemy that reproached me; then I could have borne it: neither was it he that hated me that magnified himself against me; then I would have hid myself from him: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:13">55:13</a> But it was thou, a man my equal, my guide, and my acquaintance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:14">55:14</a> We took sweet counsel together, and walked to the house of God in company. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:15">55:15</a> Let death seize upon them, and let them go down quick into hell: for wickedness is in their dwellings, and among them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:16">55:16</a> As for me, I will call upon God: and the LORD will save me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:17">55:17</a> Evening, and morning, and at noon, will I pray, and cry aloud: and he will hear my voice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:18">55:18</a> He hath delivered my soul in peace from the battle that was against me: for there were many with me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:19">55:19</a> God will hear and afflict them, even he that abideth of old. Selah. Because they have no changes, therefore they fear not God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:20">55:20</a> He hath put forth his hands against such as are at peace with him: he hath broken his covenant. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:21">55:21</a> The words of his mouth were smoother than butter, but war was in his heart: his words were softer than oil, yet were they drawn swords. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:22">55:22</a> Cast thy burden upon the LORD, and he will sustain thee: he will never suffer the righteous to be moved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:23">55:23</a> But thou, O God, wilt bring them down into the pit of destruction: bloody and deceitful men shall not live out half their days; but I will trust in thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:1">56:1</a> To the chief Musician upon Jonathelem-rechokim, Michtam of David, when the Philistines took him in Gath. Be merciful to me, O God: for man would swallow me up; he fighting daily oppresseth me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:2">56:2</a> My enemies would daily swallow me up: for they are many that fight against me, O thou Most High. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:3">56:3</a> In the time when I am afraid, I will trust in thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:4">56:4</a> In God I will praise his word, in God I have put my trust; I will not fear what flesh can do to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:5">56:5</a> Every day they wrest my words: all their thoughts are against me for evil. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:6">56:6</a> They assemble themselves, they hide themselves, they mark my steps, when they wait for my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:7">56:7</a> Shall they escape by iniquity; in thy anger cast down the people, O God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:8">56:8</a> Thou numberest my wanderings: put thou my tears into thy bottle: are they not in thy book? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:9">56:9</a> When I cry to thee, then shall my enemies turn back: this I know; for God is for me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:10">56:10</a> In God will I praise his word: in the LORD will I praise his word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:11">56:11</a> In God have I put my trust: I will not be afraid what man can do to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:12">56:12</a> Thy vows are upon me, O God: I will render praises to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:13">56:13</a> For thou hast delivered my soul from death: wilt thou not deliver my feet from falling, that I may walk before God in the light of the living? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:1">57:1</a> To the chief Musician, Al-taschith, Michtam of David, when he fled from Saul in the cave. Be merciful to me, O God, be merciful to me: for my soul trusteth in thee: yes, in the shadow of thy wings will I make my refuge, until these calamities are overpast. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:2">57:2</a> I will cry to God most high; to God that performeth all things for me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:3">57:3</a> He shall send from heaven, and save me from the reproach of him that would swallow me up. Selah. God shall send forth his mercy and his truth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:4">57:4</a> My soul is among lions: and I lie even among them that are set on fire, even the sons of men, whose teeth are spears and arrows, and their tongue a sharp sword. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:5">57:5</a> Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens; let thy glory be above all the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:6">57:6</a> They have prepared a net for my steps; my soul is bowed down: they have digged a pit before me, into the midst of which they have fallen themselves. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:7">57:7</a> My heart is fixed, O God, my heart is fixed: I will sing and give praise. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:8">57:8</a> Awake, my glory; awake, psaltery and harp: I myself will awake early. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:9">57:9</a> I will praise thee, O Lord, among the people: I will sing to thee among the nations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:10">57:10</a> For thy mercy is great to the heavens, and thy truth to the clouds. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:11">57:11</a> Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens: let thy glory be above all the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:1">58:1</a> To the chief Musician, Al-taschith, Michtam of David. Do ye indeed speak righteousness, O congregation? do ye judge uprightly, O ye sons of men? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:2">58:2</a> Yes, in heart ye work wickedness; ye weigh the violence of your hands in the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:3">58:3</a> The wicked are estranged from their birth: they go astray as soon as they are born, speaking lies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:4">58:4</a> Their poison is like the poison of a serpent: they are like the deaf adder that stoppeth her ear; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:5">58:5</a> Which will not hearken to the voice of charmers, charming never so wisely. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:6">58:6</a> Break their teeth, O God, in their mouth: break out the great teeth of the young lions, O LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:7">58:7</a> Let them melt away as waters which run continually: when he bendeth his bow to shoot his arrows, let them be as cut in pieces. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:8">58:8</a> As a snail which melteth, let every one of them pass away: like the untimely birth of a woman, that they may not see the sun. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:9">58:9</a> Before your pots can feel the thorns, he shall take them away as with a whirlwind, both living, and in his wrath. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:10">58:10</a> The righteous shall rejoice when he seeth the vengeance: he shall wash his feet in the blood of the wicked. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:11">58:11</a> So that a man shall say, Verily there is a reward for the righteous: verily he is a God that judgeth in the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:1">59:1</a> To the chief Musician, Al-taschith, Michtam of David; when Saul sent, and they watched the house to kill him. Deliver me from my enemies, O my God: defend me from them that rise up against me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:2">59:2</a> Deliver me from the workers of iniquity, and save me from bloody men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:3">59:3</a> For lo, they lie in wait for my soul: the mighty are gathered against me; not for my transgression, nor for my sin, O LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:4">59:4</a> They run and prepare themselves without my fault: awake to help me, and behold. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:5">59:5</a> Thou therefore, O LORD God of hosts, the God of Israel, awake to visit all the heathen: be not merciful to any wicked transgressors. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:6">59:6</a> They return at evening: they make a noise like a dog, and go about the city. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:7">59:7</a> Behold, they belch out with their mouth: swords are in their lips: for who, say they, doth hear? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:8">59:8</a> But thou, O LORD, shalt laugh at them; thou shalt have all the heathen in derision. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:9">59:9</a> Because of his strength will I wait upon thee: for God is my defense. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:10">59:10</a> The God of my mercy will succor me: God will let me see my desire upon my enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:11">59:11</a> Slay them not, lest my people forget: scatter them by thy power; and bring them down, O Lord our shield. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:12">59:12</a> For the sin of their mouth and the words of their lips let them even be taken in their pride: and for cursing and lying which they speak. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:13">59:13</a> Consume them in wrath, consume them, that they may not be: and let them know that God ruleth in Jacob to the ends of the earth. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:14">59:14</a> And at evening let them return; and let them make a noise like a dog, and go about the city. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:15">59:15</a> Let them wander up and down for food, and grudge if they are not satisfied. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:16">59:16</a> But I will sing of thy power; yes, I will sing aloud of thy mercy in the morning: for thou hast been my defense and refuge in the day of my trouble. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:17">59:17</a> To thee, O my strength, will I sing: for God is my defense, and the God of my mercy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:1">60:1</a> To the chief Musician upon Shushan-eduth, Michtam of David, to teach; when he strove with Aram-naharaim and with Aram-zobah, when Joab returned, and smote of Edom in the valley of salt twelve thousand. O God, thou hast cast us off, thou hast scattered us, thou hast been displeased; O turn thyself to us again. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:2">60:2</a> Thou hast made the earth to tremble; thou hast broken it: heal its breaches; for it shaketh. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:3">60:3</a> Thou hast shown thy people hard things: thou hast made us to drink the wine of astonishment. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:4">60:4</a> Thou hast given a banner to them that fear thee, that it may be displayed because of the truth. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:5">60:5</a> That thy beloved may be delivered; save with thy right hand, and hear me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:6">60:6</a> God hath spoken in his holiness; I will rejoice, I will divide Shechem, and measure out the valley of Succoth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:7">60:7</a> Gilead is mine, and Manasseh is mine; Ephraim also is the strength of my head; Judah is my lawgiver; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:8">60:8</a> Moab is my washpot; over Edom will I cast out my shoe: Philistia, triumph thou because of me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:9">60:9</a> Who will bring me into the strong city? who will lead me into Edom? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:10">60:10</a> Wilt thou not, O God, who hadst cast us off? and thou, O God, who didst not go out with our armies? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:11">60:11</a> Give us help from trouble: for vain is the help of man. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:12">60:12</a> Through God we shall do valiantly: for he will tread down our enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:1">61:1</a> To the chief Musician upon Neginah, A Psalm of David. Hear my cry, O God; attend to my prayer. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:2">61:2</a> From the end of the earth will I cry to thee, when my heart is overwhelmed: lead me to the rock that is higher than I. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:3">61:3</a> For thou hast been a shelter for me, and a strong tower from the enemy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:4">61:4</a> I will abide in thy tabernacle for ever: I will trust in the covert of thy wings. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:5">61:5</a> For thou, O God, hast heard my vows: thou hast given me the heritage of those that fear thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:6">61:6</a> Thou wilt prolong the king's life: and his years as many generations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:7">61:7</a> He shall abide before God for ever: O prepare mercy and truth, which may preserve him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:8">61:8</a> So will I sing praise to thy name for ever, that I may daily perform my vows. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:1">62:1</a> To the chief Musician, to Jeduthun, A Psalm of David. Truly my soul waiteth upon God: from him cometh my salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:2">62:2</a> He only is my rock and my salvation; he is my defense; I shall not be greatly moved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:3">62:3</a> How long will ye imagine mischief against a man? ye shall be slain all of you: as a bowing wall shall ye be, and as a tottering fence. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:4">62:4</a> They only consult to cast him down from his excellence: they delight in lies: they bless with their mouth, but they curse inwardly. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:5">62:5</a> My soul, wait thou only upon God; for my expectation is from him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:6">62:6</a> He only is my rock and my salvation: he is my defense; I shall not be moved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:7">62:7</a> In God is my salvation and my glory: the rock of my strength, and my refuge, is in God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:8">62:8</a> Trust in him at all times; ye people, pour out your heart before him: God is a refuge for us. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:9">62:9</a> Surely men of low degree are vanity, and men of high degree are a lie: to be laid in the balance, they are altogether lighter than vanity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:10">62:10</a> Trust not in oppression, and become not vain in robbery: if riches increase, set not your heart upon them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:11">62:11</a> God hath spoken once; twice have I heard this; that power belongeth to God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:12">62:12</a> Also to thee, O Lord, belongeth mercy: for thou renderest to every man according to his work. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:1">63:1</a> A Psalm of David, when he was in the wilderness of Judah. O God, thou art my God; early will I seek thee: my soul thirsteth for thee, my flesh longeth for thee in a dry and thirsty land, where no water is; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:2">63:2</a> To see thy power and thy glory, so as I have seen thee in the sanctuary. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:3">63:3</a> Because thy loving-kindness is better than life, my lips shall praise thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:4">63:4</a> Thus will I bless thee while I live: I will lift up my hands in thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:5">63:5</a> My soul shall be satisfied as with marrow and fatness; and my mouth shall praise thee with joyful lips: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:6">63:6</a> When I remember thee upon my bed, and meditate on thee in the night watches. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:7">63:7</a> Because thou hast been my help, therefore in the shadow of thy wings will I rejoice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:8">63:8</a> My soul followeth hard after thee: thy right hand upholdeth me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:9">63:9</a> But those that seek my soul to destroy it, shall go into the lower parts of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:10">63:10</a> They shall fall by the sword: they shall be a portion for foxes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:11">63:11</a> But the king shall rejoice in God; every one that sweareth by him shall glory: but the mouth of them that speak lies shall be stopped. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:1">64:1</a> To the chief Musician, a Psalm of David. Hear my voice, O God, in my prayer: preserve my life from fear of the enemy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:2">64:2</a> Hide me from the secret counsel of the wicked; from the insurrection of the workers of iniquity: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:3">64:3</a> Who whet their tongue like a sword, and bend their bows to shoot their arrows, even bitter words: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:4">64:4</a> That they may shoot in secret at the perfect: suddenly do they shoot at him, and fear not. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:5">64:5</a> They encourage themselves in an evil matter: they commune of laying snares privily; they say, Who will see them? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:6">64:6</a> They search out iniquities; they accomplish a diligent search: both the inward thought of every one of them, and the heart, is deep. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:7">64:7</a> But God shall shoot at them with an arrow; suddenly shall they be wounded. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:8">64:8</a> So they shall make their own tongue to fall upon themselves: all that see them shall flee away. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:9">64:9</a> And all men shall fear, and shall declare the work of God; for they shall wisely consider of his doing. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:10">64:10</a> The righteous shall be glad in the LORD, and shall trust in him; and all the upright in heart shall glory. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:1">65:1</a> To the chief Musician, A Psalm and Song of David. Praise waiteth for thee, O God, in Zion: and to thee shall the vow be performed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:2">65:2</a> O thou that hearest prayer, to thee shall all flesh come. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:3">65:3</a> Iniquities prevail against me: as for our transgressions, thou shalt purge them away. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:4">65:4</a> Blessed is the man whom thou choosest, and causest to approach to thee, that he may dwell in thy courts: we shall be satisfied with the goodness of thy house, even of thy holy temple. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:5">65:5</a> By terrible things in righteousness wilt thou answer us, O God of our salvation; who art the confidence of all the ends of the earth, and of them that are afar off upon the sea: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:6">65:6</a> Who by his strength setteth fast the mountains; being girded with power: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:7">65:7</a> Who stilleth the noise of the seas, the noise of their waves, and the tumult of the people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:8">65:8</a> They also that dwell in the uttermost parts are afraid at thy tokens: thou makest the outgoings of the morning and evening to rejoice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:9">65:9</a> Thou visitest the earth, and waterest it: thou greatly enrichest it with the river of God, which is full of water: thou preparest them corn, when thou hast so provided for it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:10">65:10</a> Thou waterest the ridges of it abundantly: thou settlest the furrows of it: thou makest it soft with showers: thou blessest the springing of it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:11">65:11</a> Thou crownest the year with thy goodness; and thy paths drop fatness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:12">65:12</a> They drop upon the pastures of the wilderness: and the little hills rejoice on every side. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:13">65:13</a> The pastures are clothed with flocks; the valleys also are covered over with corn; they shout for joy, they also sing. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:1">66:1</a> To the chief Musician, A Song or Psalm. Make a joyful noise to God, all ye lands: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:2">66:2</a> Sing forth the honor of his name: make his praise glorious. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:3">66:3</a> Say to God, How terrible art thou in thy works! through the greatness of thy power shall thy enemies submit themselves to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:4">66:4</a> All the earth shall worship thee, and shall sing to thee; they shall sing to thy name. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:5">66:5</a> Come and see the works of God: he is terrible in his doing towards the children of men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:6">66:6</a> He turned the sea into dry land: they went through the flood on foot: there we rejoiced in him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:7">66:7</a> He ruleth by his power for ever; his eyes behold the nations: let not the rebellious exalt themselves. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:8">66:8</a> O bless our God, ye people, and make the voice of his praise to be heard: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:9">66:9</a> Who holdeth our soul in life, and suffereth not our feet to be moved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:10">66:10</a> For thou, O God, hast proved us: thou hast tried us, as silver is tried. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:11">66:11</a> Thou hast brought us into the net; thou hast laid affliction upon our loins. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:12">66:12</a> Thou hast caused men to ride over our heads; we went through fire and through water: but thou broughtest us out into a wealthy place. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:13">66:13</a> I will go into thy house with burnt-offerings: I will pay thee my vows, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:14">66:14</a> Which my lips have uttered, and my mouth hath spoken, when I was in trouble. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:15">66:15</a> I will offer to thee burnt-sacrifices of fatlings, with the incense of rams; I will offer bullocks with goats. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:16">66:16</a> Come and hear, all ye that fear God, and I will declare what he hath done for my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:17">66:17</a> I cried to him with my mouth, and he was extolled with my tongue. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:18">66:18</a> If I regard iniquity in my heart, the Lord will not hear me: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:19">66:19</a> But verily God hath heard me; he hath attended to the voice of my prayer. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:20">66:20</a> Blessed be God, who hath not turned away my prayer, nor his mercy from me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:1">67:1</a> To the chief Musician on Neginoth, A Psalm or Song. God be merciful to us, and bless us; and cause his face to shine upon us. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:2">67:2</a> That thy way may be known upon earth, thy saving health among all nations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:3">67:3</a> Let the people praise thee, O God; let all the people praise thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:4">67:4</a> O let the nations be glad and sing for joy: for thou shalt judge the people righteously, and govern the nations upon earth. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:5">67:5</a> Let the people praise thee, O God; let all the people praise thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:6">67:6</a> Then shall the earth yield her increase; and God, even our own God, will bless us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:7">67:7</a> God will bless us, and all the ends of the earth shall fear him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:1">68:1</a> To the chief Musician, A Psalm or Song of David. Let God arise, let his enemies be scattered: let them also that hate him flee before him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:2">68:2</a> As smoke is driven away, so drive them away: as wax melteth before the fire, so let the wicked perish at the presence of God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:3">68:3</a> But let the righteous be glad; let them rejoice before God: yes, let them exceedingly rejoice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:4">68:4</a> Sing to God, sing praises to his name: extol him that rideth upon the heavens by his name JAH, and rejoice before him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:5">68:5</a> A father of the fatherless, and a judge of the widows, is God in his holy habitation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:6">68:6</a> God setteth the solitary in families: he bringeth out those who are bound with chains: but the rebellious dwell in a dry land. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:7">68:7</a> O God, when thou wentest forth before thy people, when thou didst march through the wilderness; Selah: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:8">68:8</a> The earth shook, the heavens also dropped at the presence of God: even Sinai itself was moved at the presence of God, the God of Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:9">68:9</a> Thou, O God, didst send a plentiful rain, by which thou didst confirm thy inheritance, when it was weary. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:10">68:10</a> Thy congregation hath dwelt therein: thou, O God, hast prepared of thy goodness for the poor. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:11">68:11</a> The Lord gave the word: great was the company of those that published it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:12">68:12</a> Kings of armies fled apace: and she that tarried at home divided the spoil. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:13">68:13</a> Though ye have lain among the pots, yet shall ye be as the wings of a dove covered with silver, and her feathers with yellow gold. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:14">68:14</a> When the Almighty scattered kings in it, it was white as snow in Salmon. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:15">68:15</a> The hill of God is as the hill of Bashan; a high hill as the hill of Bashan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:16">68:16</a> Why leap ye, ye lofty hills? this is the hill which God desireth to dwell in; yes, the LORD will dwell in it for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:17">68:17</a> The chariots of God are twenty thousand, even thousands of angels: the Lord is among them, as in Sinai, in the holy place. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:18">68:18</a> Thou hast ascended on high, thou hast led captivity captive: thou hast received gifts for men; yes, for the rebellious also, that the LORD God might dwell among them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:19">68:19</a> Blessed be the Lord, who daily loadeth us with benefits, even the God of our salvation. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:20">68:20</a> He that is our God is the God of salvation; and to GOD the Lord belong the issues from death. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:21">68:21</a> But God will wound the head of his enemies, and the hairy scalp of such one as goeth on still in his trespasses. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:22">68:22</a> The Lord said, I will bring again from Bashan, I will bring my people again from the depths of the sea. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:23">68:23</a> That thy foot may be dipped in the blood of thy enemies, and the tongue of thy dogs in the same. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:24">68:24</a> They have seen thy goings, O God; even the goings of my God, my King, in the sanctuary. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:25">68:25</a> The singers went before, the players on instruments followed after; among them were the damsels playing with timbrels. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:26">68:26</a> Bless ye God in the congregations, even the Lord, from the fountain of Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:27">68:27</a> There is little Benjamin with their ruler, the princes of Judah and their counsel, the princes of Zebulun, and the princes of Naphtali. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:28">68:28</a> Thy God hath commanded thy strength: strengthen, O God, that which thou hast wrought for us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:29">68:29</a> Because of thy temple at Jerusalem shall kings bring presents to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:30">68:30</a> Rebuke the company of spearmen, the multitude of the bulls, with the calves of the people, till every one shall submit himself with pieces of silver: scatter thou the people that delight in war. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:31">68:31</a> Princes shall come out of Egypt; Cush shall soon stretch out her hands to God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:32">68:32</a> Sing to God, ye kingdoms of the earth; O sing praises to the Lord; Selah: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:33">68:33</a> To him that rideth upon the heavens of heavens, which were of old; lo, he doth send out his voice, and that a mighty voice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:34">68:34</a> Ascribe ye strength to God: his excellence is over Israel, and his strength is in the clouds. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:35">68:35</a> O God, thou art terrible out of thy holy places: the God of Israel is he that giveth strength and power to his people. Blessed be God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:1">69:1</a> To the chief Musician upon Shoshannim, A Psalm of David. Save me, O God; for the waters are come in to my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:2">69:2</a> I sink in deep mire, where there is no standing: I am come into deep waters, where the floods overflow me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:3">69:3</a> I am weary of my crying: my throat is dried: my eyes fail while I wait for my God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:4">69:4</a> They that hate me without a cause are more than the hairs of my head: they that would destroy me, being my enemies wrongfully, are mighty: then I restored that which I took not away. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:5">69:5</a> O God, thou knowest my foolishness; and my sins are not hid from thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:6">69:6</a> Let not them that wait on thee, O Lord GOD of hosts, be ashamed for my sake: let not those that seek thee be confounded for my sake, O God of Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:7">69:7</a> Because for thy sake I have borne reproach; shame hath covered my face. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:8">69:8</a> I am become a stranger to my brethren, and an alien to my mother's children. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:9">69:9</a> For the zeal of thy house hath eaten me up; and the reproaches of them that reproached thee have fallen upon me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:10">69:10</a> When I wept, and chastened my soul with fasting, that was to my reproach. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:11">69:11</a> I made sackcloth also my garment; and I became a proverb to them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:12">69:12</a> They that sit in the gate speak against me; and I was the song of the drunkards. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:13">69:13</a> But as for me, my prayer is to thee, O LORD, in an acceptable time: O God, in the multitude of thy mercy hear me, in the truth of thy salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:14">69:14</a> Deliver me out of the mire, and let me not sink: let me be delivered from them that hate me, and out of the deep waters. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:15">69:15</a> Let not the water-flood overflow me, neither let the deep swallow me up, and let not the pit shut her mouth upon me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:16">69:16</a> Hear me, O LORD; for thy loving-kindness is good: turn to me according to the multitude of thy tender mercies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:17">69:17</a> And hide not thy face from thy servant; for I am in trouble: hear me speedily. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:18">69:18</a> Draw nigh to my soul, and redeem it: deliver me because of my enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:19">69:19</a> Thou hast known my reproach, and my shame, and my dishonor: my adversaries are all before thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:20">69:20</a> Reproach hath broken my heart; and I am full of heaviness: and I looked for some to take pity, but there was none; and for comforters, but I found none. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:21">69:21</a> They gave me also gall for my food; and in my thirst they gave me vinegar to drink. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:22">69:22</a> Let their table become a snare before them: and that which should have been for their welfare, let it become a trap. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:23">69:23</a> Let their eyes be darkened, that they see not; and make their loins continually to shake. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:24">69:24</a> Pour out thy indignation upon them, and let thy wrathful anger take hold of them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:25">69:25</a> Let their habitation be desolate; and let none dwell in their tents. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:26">69:26</a> For they persecute him whom thou hast smitten; and they talk to the grief of those whom thou hast wounded. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:27">69:27</a> Add iniquity to their iniquity: and let them not come into thy righteousness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:28">69:28</a> Let them be blotted out of the book of the living, and not be written with the righteous. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:29">69:29</a> But I am poor and sorrowful: let thy salvation, O God, set me up on high. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:30">69:30</a> I will praise the name of God with a song, and will magnify him with thanksgiving. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:31">69:31</a> This also shall please the LORD better than an ox or bullock that hath horns and hoofs. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:32">69:32</a> The humble shall see this, and be glad: and your heart shall live that seek God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:33">69:33</a> For the LORD heareth the poor, and despiseth not his prisoners. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:34">69:34</a> Let the heaven and earth praise him, the seas, and every thing that moveth therein. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:35">69:35</a> For God will save Zion, and will build the cities of Judah: that they may dwell there, and have it in possession. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:36">69:36</a> The seed also of his servants shall inherit it: and they that love his name shall dwell therein. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:1">70:1</a> To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David to bring to remembrance. Make haste, O God, to deliver me; make haste to help me, O LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:2">70:2</a> Let them be ashamed and confounded that seek after my soul: let them be turned backward, and put to confusion, that desire my hurt. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:3">70:3</a> Let them be turned back for a reward of their shame that say, Aha, aha. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:4">70:4</a> Let all those that seek thee rejoice and be glad in thee: and let such as love thy salvation say continually, Let God be magnified. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:5">70:5</a> But I am poor and needy: make haste to me, O God: thou art my help and my deliverer; O LORD, make no delay. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:1">71:1</a> In thee, O LORD, do I put my trust: let me never be put to confusion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:2">71:2</a> Deliver me in thy righteousness, and cause me to escape: incline thy ear to me, and save me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:3">71:3</a> Be thou my strong habitation, to which I may continually resort: thou hast given commandment to save me; for thou art my rock and my fortress. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:4">71:4</a> Deliver me, O my God, from the hand of the wicked, from the hand of the unrighteous and cruel man. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:5">71:5</a> For thou art my hope, O Lord GOD: thou art my trust from my youth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:6">71:6</a> By thee have I been sustained from my birth: thou art he that brought me into life: my praise shall be continually of thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:7">71:7</a> I am as a wonder to many; but thou art my strong refuge. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:8">71:8</a> Let my mouth be filled with thy praise and with thy honor all the day. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:9">71:9</a> Cast me not off in the time of old age; forsake me not when my strength faileth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:10">71:10</a> For my enemies speak against me; and they that lay wait for my soul take counsel together, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:11">71:11</a> Saying, God hath forsaken him: persecute and take him; for there is none to deliver him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:12">71:12</a> O God, be not far from me: O my God, make haste for my help. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:13">71:13</a> Let them be confounded and consumed that are adversaries to my soul; let them be covered with reproach and dishonor that seek my hurt. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:14">71:14</a> But I will hope continually, and will yet praise thee more and more. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:15">71:15</a> My mouth shall show forth thy righteousness and thy salvation all the day; for I know not the numbers thereof. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:16">71:16</a> I will go in the strength of the Lord GOD: I will make mention of thy righteousness, even of thine only. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:17">71:17</a> O God, thou hast taught me from my youth: and hitherto have I declared thy wondrous works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:18">71:18</a> Now also when I am old and gray-headed, O God, forsake me not; until I have shown thy strength to this generation, and thy power to every one that is to come. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:19">71:19</a> Thy righteousness also, O God, is very high, who hast done great things: O God, who is like to thee! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:20">71:20</a> Thou, who hast shown me great and severe troubles, wilt revive me again, and wilt bring me again from the depths of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:21">71:21</a> Thou wilt increase my greatness, and comfort me on every side. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:22">71:22</a> I will also praise thee with the psaltery, even thy truth, O my God: to thee will I sing with the harp, O thou Holy One of Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:23">71:23</a> My lips shall greatly rejoice when I sing to thee; and my soul, which thou hast redeemed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:24">71:24</a> My tongue also shall talk of thy righteousness all the day long: for they are confounded, for they are brought to shame, that seek my hurt. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:1">72:1</a> A Psalm for Solomon. Give the king thy judgments, O God, and thy righteousness to the king's son. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:2">72:2</a> He shall judge thy people with righteousness, and thy poor with judgment. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:3">72:3</a> The mountains shall bring peace to the people, and the little hills, by righteousness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:4">72:4</a> He shall judge the poor of the people, he shall save the children of the needy, and shall break in pieces the oppressor. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:5">72:5</a> They shall fear thee as long as the sun and moon endure, throughout all generations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:6">72:6</a> He shall come down like rain upon the mown grass: as showers that water the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:7">72:7</a> In his days shall the righteous flourish; and abundance of peace so long as the moon endureth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:8">72:8</a> He shall have dominion also from sea to sea, and from the river to the ends of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:9">72:9</a> They that dwell in the wilderness shall bow before him; and his enemies shall lick the dust. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:10">72:10</a> The kings of Tarshish and of the isles shall bring presents: the kings of Sheba and Seba shall offer gifts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:11">72:11</a> Yes, all kings shall fall down before him: all nations shall serve him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:12">72:12</a> For he shall deliver the needy when he crieth; the poor also, and him that hath no helper. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:13">72:13</a> He shall spare the poor and needy, and shall save the souls of the needy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:14">72:14</a> He shall redeem their soul from deceit and violence: and precious shall be their blood in his sight. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:15">72:15</a> And he shall live, and to him shall be given of the gold of Sheba: prayer also shall be made for him continually; and daily shall he be praised. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:16">72:16</a> There shall be a handful of corn in the earth upon the top of the mountains; the fruit of it shall shake like Lebanon: and they of the city shall flourish like grass of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:17">72:17</a> His name shall endure for ever: his name shall be continued as long as the sun: and men shall be blessed in him: all nations shall call him blessed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:18">72:18</a> Blessed be the LORD God, the God of Israel, who only doeth wondrous things. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:19">72:19</a> And blessed be his glorious name for ever: and let the whole earth be filled with his glory; Amen, and amen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:20">72:20</a> The prayers of David the son of Jesse are ended. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:1">73:1</a> A Psalm of Asaph. Truly God is good to Israel, even to such as are of a clean heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:2">73:2</a> But as for me, my feet were almost gone; my steps had well nigh slipped. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:3">73:3</a> For I was envious at the foolish, when I saw the prosperity of the wicked. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:4">73:4</a> For there are no bands in their death: but their strength is firm. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:5">73:5</a> They are not in trouble as other men; neither are they afflicted like other men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:6">73:6</a> Therefore pride encompasseth them as a chain; violence covereth them as a garment. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:7">73:7</a> Their eyes stand out with fatness: they have more than heart could wish. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:8">73:8</a> They are corrupt, and speak wickedly concerning oppression: they speak loftily. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:9">73:9</a> They set their mouth against the heavens, and their tongue walketh through the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:10">73:10</a> Therefore his people return hither: and waters of a full cup are wrung out to them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:11">73:11</a> And they say, How doth God know? and is there knowledge in the Most High? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:12">73:12</a> Behold, these are the ungodly, who prosper in the world; they increase in riches. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:13">73:13</a> Verily I have cleansed my heart in vain, and washed my hands in innocence. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:14">73:14</a> For all the day long have I been afflicted, and chastened every morning. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:15">73:15</a> If I say, I will speak thus; behold, I should offend against the generation of thy children. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:16">73:16</a> When I thought to know this, it was too painful for me; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:17">73:17</a> Until I went into the sanctuary of God; then I understood their end. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:18">73:18</a> Surely thou didst set them in slippery places: thou didst cast them down into destruction. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:19">73:19</a> How are they brought into desolation, as in a moment! they are utterly consumed with terrors. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:20">73:20</a> As a dream when one awaketh; so, O Lord, when thou awakest, thou wilt despise their image. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:21">73:21</a> Thus my heart was grieved, and I was pricked in my reins. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:22">73:22</a> So foolish was I, and ignorant: I was as a beast before thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:23">73:23</a> Nevertheless I am continually with thee: thou hast held me by my right hand. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:24">73:24</a> Thou wilt guide me with thy counsel, and afterward receive me to glory. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:25">73:25</a> Whom have I in heaven but thee? and there is none upon earth that I desire besides thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:26">73:26</a> My flesh and my heart faileth: but God is the strength of my heart, and my portion for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:27">73:27</a> For lo, they that are far from thee shall perish: thou hast destroyed all them that go astray from thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:28">73:28</a> But it is good for me to draw near to God: I have put my trust in the Lord GOD, that I may declare all thy works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:1">74:1</a> Maschil of Asaph. O God, why hast thou cast us off for ever? why doth thy anger smoke against the sheep of thy pasture? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:2">74:2</a> Remember thy congregation, which thou hast purchased of old: the rod of thy inheritance, which thou hast redeemed; this mount Zion, in which thou hast dwelt. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:3">74:3</a> Lift up thy feet to the perpetual desolations; even all that the enemy hath done wickedly in the sanctuary. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:4">74:4</a> Thy enemies roar in the midst of thy congregations; they set up their ensigns for signs. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:5">74:5</a> A man was famous according as he had lifted up axes upon the thick trees. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:6">74:6</a> But now they break down the carved work of it at once with axes and hammers. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:7">74:7</a> They have cast fire into thy sanctuary, they have defiled by casting down the dwelling-place of thy name to the ground. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:8">74:8</a> They said in their hearts, Let us destroy them together: they have burned up all the synagogues of God in the land. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:9">74:9</a> We see not our signs: there is no more any prophet: neither is there among us any that knoweth how long. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:10">74:10</a> O God, how long shall the adversary reproach? shall the enemy blaspheme thy name for ever? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:11">74:11</a> Why withdrawest thou thy hand, even thy right hand? pluck it out of thy bosom. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:12">74:12</a> For God is my King of old, working salvation in the midst of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:13">74:13</a> Thou didst divide the sea by thy strength: thou didst break the heads of the dragons in the waters. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:14">74:14</a> Thou didst break the head of leviathan in pieces, and didst give him to be food to the people inhabiting the wilderness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:15">74:15</a> Thou didst cleave the fountain and the flood: thou didst dry up mighty rivers. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:16">74:16</a> The day is thine, the night also is thine: thou hast prepared the light and the sun. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:17">74:17</a> Thou hast set all the borders of the earth: thou hast made summer and winter. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:18">74:18</a> Remember this, the enemy hath reproached, O LORD, and the foolish people have blasphemed thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:19">74:19</a> O deliver not the soul of thy turtle dove to the multitude of the wicked: forget not the congregation of thy poor for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:20">74:20</a> Have respect to the covenant: for the dark places of the earth are full of the habitations of cruelty. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:21">74:21</a> O let not the oppressed return ashamed: let the poor and needy praise thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:22">74:22</a> Arise, O God, plead thy own cause: remember how the foolish man reproacheth thee daily. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:23">74:23</a> Forget not the voice of thy enemies: the tumult of those that rise against thee increaseth continually. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:1">75:1</a> To the chief Musician, Al-taschith, A Psalm or Song of Asaph. To thee, O God, do we give thanks, to thee do we give thanks: for that thy name is near, thy wondrous works declare. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:2">75:2</a> When I shall receive the congregation I will judge uprightly. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:3">75:3</a> The earth and all its inhabitants are dissolved: I bear up the pillars of it. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:4">75:4</a> I said to the fools, Deal not foolishly; and to the wicked, Lift not up the horn: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:5">75:5</a> Lift not up your horn on high: speak not with a stiff neck. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:6">75:6</a> For promotion cometh neither from the east, nor from the west, nor from the south. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:7">75:7</a> But God is the judge: he putteth down one, and setteth up another. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:8">75:8</a> For in the hand of the LORD there is a cup, and the wine is red; it is full of mixture, and he poureth out of the same: but the dregs of it all the wicked of the earth shall wring them out, and drink them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:9">75:9</a> But I will declare for ever; I will sing praises to the God of Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:10">75:10</a> All the horns of the wicked also will I cut off; but the horns of the righteous shall be exalted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:1">76:1</a> To the chief Musician on Neginoth, A Psalm or Song of Asaph. In Judah is God known: his name is great in Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:2">76:2</a> In Salem also is his tabernacle, and his dwelling place in Zion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:3">76:3</a> There he broke the arrows of the bow, the shield, and the sword, and the battle. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:4">76:4</a> Thou art more glorious and excellent than the mountains of prey. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:5">76:5</a> The stout-hearted are spoiled, they have slept their sleep: and none of the men of might have found their hands. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:6">76:6</a> At thy rebuke, O God of Jacob, both the chariot and horse are cast into a dead sleep. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:7">76:7</a> Thou, even thou, art to be feared: and who may stand in thy sight when once thou art angry? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:8">76:8</a> Thou didst cause judgment to be heard from heaven; the earth feared, and was still, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:9">76:9</a> When God arose to judgment, to save all the meek of the earth. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:10">76:10</a> Surely the wrath of man shall praise thee: the remainder of wrath wilt thou restrain. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:11">76:11</a> Vow, and pay to the LORD your God: let all that are about him bring presents to him that ought to be feared. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:12">76:12</a> He shall cut off the spirit of princes: he is terrible to the kings of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:1">77:1</a> To the chief Musician, to Jeduthun, A Psalm of Asaph. I cried to God with my voice, even to God with my voice; and he gave ear to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:2">77:2</a> In the day of my trouble I sought the Lord: my sore ran in the night, and ceased not: my soul refused to be comforted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:3">77:3</a> I remembered God, and was troubled: I complained, and my spirit was overwhelmed. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:4">77:4</a> Thou holdest my eyes waking: I am so troubled that I cannot speak. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:5">77:5</a> I have considered the days of old, the years of ancient times. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:6">77:6</a> I call to remembrance my song in the night: I commune with my own heart: and my spirit made diligent search. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:7">77:7</a> Will the Lord cast off for ever? and will he be favorable no more? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:8">77:8</a> Is his mercy wholly gone for ever? doth his promise fail for evermore? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:9">77:9</a> Hath God forgotten to be gracious? hath he in anger shut up his tender mercies? Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:10">77:10</a> And I said, This is my infirmity: but I will remember the years of the right hand of the Most High. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:11">77:11</a> I will remember the works of the LORD: surely I will remember thy wonders of old. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:12">77:12</a> I will meditate also of all thy work, and talk of thy doings. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:13">77:13</a> Thy way, O God, is in the sanctuary: who is so great a God as our God! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:14">77:14</a> Thou art the God that doest wonders: thou hast declared thy strength among the people. </p>
