 <p><a name="an_77:15">77:15</a> Thou hast with thy arm redeemed thy people, the sons of Jacob and Joseph. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:16">77:16</a> The waters saw thee, O God, the waters saw thee; they were afraid: the depths also were disturbed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:17">77:17</a> The clouds poured out water: the skies sent out a sound: thy arrows also went abroad. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:18">77:18</a> The voice of thy thunder was in the heaven: the lightnings lightened the world: the earth trembled and shook. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:19">77:19</a> Thy way is in the sea, and thy path in the great waters, and thy footsteps are not known. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:20">77:20</a> Thou leddest thy people like a flock by the hand of Moses and Aaron. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:1">78:1</a> Maschil of Asaph. Give ear, O my people, to my law: incline your ear to the words of my mouth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:2">78:2</a> I will open my mouth in a parable: I will utter dark sayings of old: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:3">78:3</a> Which we have heard and known, and our fathers have told us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:4">78:4</a> We will not hide them from their children, showing to the generation to come the praises of the LORD, and his strength, and his wonderful works that he hath done. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:5">78:5</a> For he established a testimony in Jacob, and appointed a law in Israel, which he commanded our fathers, that they should make them known to their children: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:6">78:6</a> That the generation to come might know them, even the children who should be born; who should arise and declare them to their children: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:7">78:7</a> That they might set their hope in God, and not forget the works of God, but keep his commandments: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:8">78:8</a> And might not be as their fathers, a stubborn and rebellious generation; a generation that set not their heart aright, and whose spirit was not steadfast with God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:9">78:9</a> The children of Ephraim, being armed, and carrying bows, turned back in the day of battle. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:10">78:10</a> They kept not the covenant of God, and refused to walk in his law; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:11">78:11</a> And forgot his works, and his wonders that he had shown them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:12">78:12</a> Marvelous things did he in the sight of their fathers, in the land of Egypt, in the field of Zoan. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:13">78:13</a> He divided the sea, and caused them to pass through; and he made the waters to stand as a heap. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:14">78:14</a> In the day-time also he led them with a cloud, and all the night with a light of fire. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:15">78:15</a> He cleaved the rocks in the wilderness, and gave them drink as out of the great depths. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:16">78:16</a> He brought streams also out of the rock, and caused waters to run down like rivers. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:17">78:17</a> And they sinned yet more against him by provoking the Most High in the wilderness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:18">78:18</a> And they tempted God in their heart by asking food for their desire. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:19">78:19</a> Yes, they spoke against God; they said, Can God furnish a table in the wilderness? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:20">78:20</a> Behold, he smote the rock, that the waters gushed out, and the streams overflowed; can he give bread also? can he provide flesh for his people? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:21">78:21</a> Therefore the LORD heard this, and was wroth: so a fire was kindled against Jacob, and anger also came up against Israel; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:22">78:22</a> Because they believed not in God, and trusted not in his salvation: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:23">78:23</a> Though he had commanded the clouds from above, and opened the doors of heaven, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:24">78:24</a> And had rained down manna upon them to eat, and had given them of the corn of heaven. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:25">78:25</a> Man ate angels' food: he sent them food to the full. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:26">78:26</a> He caused an east wind to blow in the heaven: and by his power he brought in the south wind. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:27">78:27</a> He rained flesh also upon them as dust, and feathered fowls like as the sand of the sea: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:28">78:28</a> And he let it fall in the midst of their camp, around their habitations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:29">78:29</a> So they ate, and were well filled: for he gave them their own desire; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:30">78:30</a> They were not estranged from their desire: but while their meat was yet in their mouths, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:31">78:31</a> The wrath of God came upon them, and slew the fattest of them, and smote down the chosen men of Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:32">78:32</a> For all this they sinned still, and believed not for his wondrous works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:33">78:33</a> Therefore their days did he consume in vanity, and their years in trouble. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:34">78:34</a> When he slew them, then they sought him: and they returned and inquired early after God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:35">78:35</a> And they remembered that God was their rock, and the high God their redeemer. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:36">78:36</a> Nevertheless they flattered him with their mouth, and they lied to him with their tongues. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:37">78:37</a> For their heart was not right with him, neither were they steadfast in his covenant. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:38">78:38</a> But he, being full of compassion, forgave their iniquity, and destroyed them not: yes, many a time he turned his anger away, and did not stir up all his wrath. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:39">78:39</a> For he remembered that they were but flesh; a wind that passeth away, and cometh not again. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:40">78:40</a> How oft did they provoke him in the wilderness, and grieve him in the desert! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:41">78:41</a> Yes, they turned back and tempted God, and limited the Holy One of Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:42">78:42</a> They remembered not his hand, nor the day when he delivered them from the enemy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:43">78:43</a> How he had wrought his signs in Egypt, and his wonders in the field of Zoan: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:44">78:44</a> And had turned their rivers into blood; and their floods, that they could not drink. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:45">78:45</a> He sent divers sorts of flies among them, which devoured them; and frogs, which destroyed them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:46">78:46</a> He gave also their increase to the caterpillar, and their labor to the locust. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:47">78:47</a> He destroyed their vines with hail, and their sycamore trees with frost. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:48">78:48</a> He gave up their cattle also to the hail, and their flocks to hot thunderbolts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:49">78:49</a> He cast upon them the fierceness of his anger, wrath, and indignation, and trouble, by sending evil angels among them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:50">78:50</a> He made a way to his anger; he spared not their soul from death, but gave their life over to the pestilence; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:51">78:51</a> And smote all the first-born in Egypt; the chief of their strength in the tabernacles of Ham: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:52">78:52</a> But made his own people to go forth like sheep, and guided them in the wilderness like a flock. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:53">78:53</a> And he led them on safely, so that they feared not: but the sea overwhelmed their enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:54">78:54</a> And he brought them to the border of his sanctuary, even to this mountain, which his right hand had purchased. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:55">78:55</a> He cast out the heathen also before them, and divided them an inheritance by line, and made the tribes of Israel to dwell in their tents. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:56">78:56</a> Yet they tempted and provoked the most high God, and kept not his testimonies: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:57">78:57</a> But turned back, and dealt unfaithfully like their fathers: they were turned aside like a deceitful bow. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:58">78:58</a> For they provoked him to anger with their high places, and moved him to jealousy with their graven images. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:59">78:59</a> When God heard this, he was wroth, and greatly abhorred Israel: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:60">78:60</a> So that he forsook the tabernacle of Shiloh, the tent which he placed among men; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:61">78:61</a> And delivered his strength into captivity, and his glory into the enemy's hand. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:62">78:62</a> He gave over his people also to the sword; and was wroth with his inheritance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:63">78:63</a> The fire consumed their young men; and their maidens were not given to marriage. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:64">78:64</a> Their priests fell by the sword; and their widows made no lamentation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:65">78:65</a> Then the Lord awaked as one out of sleep, and like a mighty man that shouteth by reason of wine. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:66">78:66</a> And he smote his enemies in the hinder part: he put them to a perpetual reproach. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:67">78:67</a> Moreover he refused the tabernacle of Joseph, and chose not the tribe of Ephraim: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:68">78:68</a> But chose the tribe of Judah, the mount Zion which he loved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:69">78:69</a> And he built his sanctuary like high palaces, like the earth which he hath established for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:70">78:70</a> He chose David also his servant, and took him from the sheep-folds: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:71">78:71</a> From following the ewes great with young he brought him to feed Jacob his people, and Israel his inheritance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:72">78:72</a> So he fed them according to the integrity of his heart; and guided them by the skillfulness of his hands. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:1">79:1</a> A Psalm of Asaph. O God, the heathen have come into thy inheritance; thy holy temple have they defiled; they have laid Jerusalem on heaps. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:2">79:2</a> The dead bodies of thy servants have they given to be food to the fowls of the heaven, the flesh of thy saints, to the beasts of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:3">79:3</a> Their blood have they shed like water around Jerusalem; and there was none to bury them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:4">79:4</a> We have become a reproach to our neighbors, a scorn and derision to them that are around us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:5">79:5</a> How long, LORD? wilt thou be angry for ever? shall thy jealousy burn like fire? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:6">79:6</a> Pour out thy wrath upon the heathen that have not known thee, and upon the kingdoms that have not called upon thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:7">79:7</a> For they have devoured Jacob, and laid waste his dwelling-place. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:8">79:8</a> O remember not against us former iniquities: let thy tender mercies speedily succor us: for we are brought very low. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:9">79:9</a> Help us, O God of our salvation, for the glory of thy name: and deliver us, and purge away our sins, for thy name's sake. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:10">79:10</a> Why should the heathen say, Where is their God? let him be known among the heathen in our sight by avenging the blood of thy servants which is shed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:11">79:11</a> Let the sighing of the prisoner come before thee; according to the greatness of thy power preserve thou those that are appointed to die; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:12">79:12</a> And render to our neighbors seven-fold into their bosom their reproach, with which they have reproached thee, O Lord. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:13">79:13</a> So we thy people and sheep of thy pasture will give thee thanks for ever: we will show forth thy praise to all generations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:1">80:1</a> To the chief Musician upon Shoshannim Eduth, A Psalm of Asaph. Give ear, O Shepherd of Israel, thou that leadest Joseph like a flock; thou that dwellest between the cherubim, shine forth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:2">80:2</a> Before Ephraim and Benjamin and Manasseh stir up thy strength, and come and save us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:3">80:3</a> Turn us again, O God, and cause thy face to shine; and we shall be saved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:4">80:4</a> O LORD God of hosts, how long wilt thou be angry against the prayer of thy people? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:5">80:5</a> Thou feedest them with the bread of tears; and givest them tears to drink in great measure. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:6">80:6</a> Thou makest us a strife to our neighbors: and our enemies laugh among themselves. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:7">80:7</a> Turn us again, O God of hosts, and cause thy face to shine; and we shall be saved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:8">80:8</a> Thou hast brought a vine out of Egypt: thou hast cast out the heathen, and planted it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:9">80:9</a> Thou preparedst room before it, and didst cause it to take deep root, and it filled the land. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:10">80:10</a> The hills were covered with the shade of it, and its boughs were like the goodly cedars. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:11">80:11</a> She sent out her boughs to the sea, and her branches to the river. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:12">80:12</a> Why hast thou then broke down her hedges, so that all they who pass by the way do pluck her? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:13">80:13</a> The boar from the wood doth waste it, and the wild beast of the field doth devour it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:14">80:14</a> Return, we beseech thee, O God of hosts: look down from heaven, and behold, and visit this vine; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:15">80:15</a> And the vineyard which thy right hand planted, and the branch that thou madest strong for thyself. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:16">80:16</a> It is burnt with fire, it is cut down: they perish at the rebuke of thy countenance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:17">80:17</a> Let thy hand be upon the man of thy right hand, upon the son of man whom thou madest strong for thyself. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:18">80:18</a> So will we not go back from thee: revive us, and we will call upon thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:19">80:19</a> Turn us again, O LORD God of hosts, cause thy face to shine; and we shall be saved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:1">81:1</a> To the chief Musician upon Gittith, A Psalm  of Asaph. Sing aloud to God our strength: make a joyful noise to the God of Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:2">81:2</a> Take a psalm, and bring hither the timbrel, the pleasant harp with the psaltery. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:3">81:3</a> Blow the trumpet in the new moon, in the time appointed, on our solemn feast day. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:4">81:4</a> For this was a statute for Israel, and a law of the God of Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:5">81:5</a> This he ordained in Joseph for a testimony, when he went out through the land of Egypt: where I heard a language that I understood not. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:6">81:6</a> I removed his shoulder from the burden: his hands were delivered from the pots. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:7">81:7</a> Thou calledst in trouble, and I delivered thee; I answered thee in the secret place of thunder: I proved thee at the waters of Meribah. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:8">81:8</a> Hear, O my people, and I will testify to thee; O Israel, if thou wilt hearken to me; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:9">81:9</a> There shall no strange god be in thee; neither shalt thou worship any strange god. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:10">81:10</a> I am the LORD thy God who brought thee out of the land of Egypt: open thy mouth wide, and I will fill it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:11">81:11</a> But my people would not hearken to my voice; and Israel would not obey me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:12">81:12</a> So I gave them up to their own hearts lust: and they walked in their own counsels. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:13">81:13</a> O that my people had hearkened to me, and Israel had walked in my ways! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:14">81:14</a> I should soon have subdued their enemies, and turned my hand against their adversaries. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:15">81:15</a> The haters of the LORD should have submitted themselves to him: and their time should have endured for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:16">81:16</a> He would have fed them also with the finest of the wheat: and with honey out of the rock I should have satisfied thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:1">82:1</a> A Psalm of Asaph. God standeth in the congregation of the mighty; he judgeth among the gods. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:2">82:2</a> How long will ye judge unjustly, and accept the persons of the wicked? Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:3">82:3</a> Defend the poor and fatherless: do justice to the afflicted and needy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:4">82:4</a> Deliver the poor and needy: deliver them from the hand of the wicked. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:5">82:5</a> They know not, neither will they understand; they walk on in darkness: all the foundations of the earth are out of course. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:6">82:6</a> I have said, Ye are gods; and all of you are children of the Most High. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:7">82:7</a> But ye shall die like men, and fall like one of the princes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:8">82:8</a> Arise, O God, judge the earth: for thou wilt inherit all nations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:1">83:1</a> A song, or Psalm of Asaph. Keep not thou silence, O God: hold not thy peace, and be not still, O God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:2">83:2</a> For lo, thy enemies make a tumult: and they that hate thee have lifted up the head. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:3">83:3</a> They have taken crafty counsel against thy people, and consulted against thy hidden ones. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:4">83:4</a> They have said, Come, and let us cut them off from being a nation; that the name of Israel may be no more in remembrance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:5">83:5</a> For they have consulted together with one consent: they are confederate against thee, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:6">83:6</a> The tabernacles of Edom, and the Ishmaelites; of Moab, and the Hagarenes; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:7">83:7</a> Gebal, and Ammon, and Amalek; the Philistines with the inhabitants of Tyre; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:8">83:8</a> Assur also is joined with them: they have helped the children of Lot. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:9">83:9</a> Do to them as to the Midianites; as to Sisera, as to Jabin, at the brook of Kison: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:10">83:10</a> Who perished at En-dor: they became as dung for the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:11">83:11</a> Make their nobles like Oreb, and like Zeeb: yes, all their princes as Zebah, and as Zalmunna: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:12">83:12</a> Who said, Let us take to ourselves the houses of God in possession. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:13">83:13</a> O my God, make them like a wheel; as the stubble before the wind. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:14">83:14</a> As the fire burneth a wood, and as the flame setteth the mountains on fire; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:15">83:15</a> So persecute them with thy tempest, and make them afraid with thy storm. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:16">83:16</a> Fill their faces with shame; that they may seek thy name, O LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:17">83:17</a> Let them be confounded and troubled for ever; yes, let them be put to shame, and perish: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:18">83:18</a> That men may know that thou, whose name alone is JEHOVAH, art the most high over all the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:1">84:1</a> To the chief Musician upon Gittith, A Psalm for the sons of Korah. How amiable are thy tabernacles, O LORD of hosts! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:2">84:2</a> My soul longeth, and even fainteth for the courts of the LORD: my heart and my flesh crieth out for the living God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:3">84:3</a> Yes, the sparrow hath found a house, and the swallow a nest for herself, where she may lay her young, even thy altars, O LORD of hosts, my King, and my God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:4">84:4</a> Blessed are they that dwell in thy house: they will be still praising thee. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:5">84:5</a> Blessed is the man whose strength is in thee; in whose heart are the ways of them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:6">84:6</a> Who passing through the valley of Baca make it a well; the rain also filleth the pools. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:7">84:7</a> They go from strength to strength, every one of them in Zion appeareth before God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:8">84:8</a> O LORD God of hosts, hear my prayer: give ear, O God of Jacob. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:9">84:9</a> Behold, O God our shield, and look upon the face of thy anointed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:10">84:10</a> For a day in thy courts is better than a thousand. I had rather be a door-keeper in the house of my God, than to dwell in the tents of wickedness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:11">84:11</a> For the LORD God is a sun and shield: the LORD will give grace and glory: no good will he withhold from them that walk uprightly. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:12">84:12</a> O LORD of hosts, blessed is the man that trusteth in thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:1">85:1</a> To the chief Musician, A Psalm for the sons of Korah. LORD, thou hast been favorable to thy land: thou hast brought back the captivity of Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:2">85:2</a> Thou hast forgiven the iniquity of thy people, thou hast covered all their sin. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:3">85:3</a> Thou hast taken away all thy wrath; thou hast turned thyself from the fierceness of thy anger. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:4">85:4</a> Turn us, O God of our salvation, and cause thy anger towards us to cease. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:5">85:5</a> Wilt thou be angry with us for ever? wilt thou draw out thy anger to all generations? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:6">85:6</a> Wilt thou not revive us again: that thy people may rejoice in thee? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:7">85:7</a> Show us thy mercy, O LORD, and grant us thy salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:8">85:8</a> I will hear what God the LORD will speak: for he will speak peace to his people, and to his saints: but let them not turn again to folly. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:9">85:9</a> Surely his salvation is nigh them that fear him; that glory may dwell in our land. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:10">85:10</a> Mercy and truth are met together; righteousness and peace have kissed each other. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:11">85:11</a> Truth shall spring out of the earth; and righteousness shall look down from heaven. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:12">85:12</a> Yes, the LORD will give that which is good; and our land shall yield her increase. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:13">85:13</a> Righteousness shall go before him; and shall set us in the way of his steps. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:1">86:1</a> A Prayer of David. Bow down thy ear, O LORD, hear me: for I am poor and needy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:2">86:2</a> Preserve my soul; for I am holy: O thou my God, save thy servant that trusteth in thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:3">86:3</a> Be merciful to me, O Lord: for I cry to thee daily. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:4">86:4</a> Rejoice the soul of thy servant: for to thee, O Lord, do I lift up my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:5">86:5</a> For thou, Lord, art good, and ready to forgive; and abundant in mercy to all them that call upon thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:6">86:6</a> Give ear, O LORD, to my prayer; and attend to the voice of my supplications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:7">86:7</a> In the day of my trouble I will call upon thee: for thou wilt answer me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:8">86:8</a> Among the gods there is none like thee, O Lord; neither are there any works like thy works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:9">86:9</a> All nations whom thou hast made shall come and worship before thee, O Lord; and shall glorify thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:10">86:10</a> For thou art great, and doest wondrous things: thou art God alone. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:11">86:11</a> Teach me thy way, O LORD; I will walk in thy truth: unite my heart to fear thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:12">86:12</a> I will praise thee, O Lord my God, with all my heart: and I will glorify thy name for evermore. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:13">86:13</a> For great is thy mercy towards me: and thou hast delivered my soul from the lowest hell. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:14">86:14</a> O God, the proud have risen against me, and the assemblies of violent men have sought after my soul; and have not set thee before them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:15">86:15</a> But thou, O Lord, art a God full of compassion, and gracious; long-suffering, and abundant in mercy and truth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:16">86:16</a> O turn to me, and have mercy upon me; give thy strength to thy servant, and save the son of thy handmaid. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:17">86:17</a> Show me a token for good; that they who hate me may see it, and be ashamed: because thou, LORD, hast helped me, and comforted me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:1">87:1</a> A Psalm or Song for the sons of Korah. His foundation is in the holy mountains. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:2">87:2</a> The LORD loveth the gates of Zion more than all the dwellings of Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:3">87:3</a> Glorious things are spoken of thee, O city of God. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:4">87:4</a> I will make mention of Rahab and Babylon to them that know me: behold Philistia, and Tyre, with Cush; this man was born there. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:5">87:5</a> And of Zion it shall be said, This and that man was born in her: and the Highest himself shall establish her. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:6">87:6</a> The LORD shall count, when he writeth up the people, that this man was born there. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:7">87:7</a> As well the singers as the players on instruments shall be there: all my springs are in thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:1">88:1</a> A Song or Psalm for the sons of Korah, to the chief Musician upon Mahalath Leannoth, Maschil of Heman the Ezrahite. O LORD God of my salvation, I have cried day and night before thee: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:2">88:2</a> Let my prayer come before thee: incline thy ear to my cry; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:3">88:3</a> For my soul is full of troubles: and my life draweth nigh to the grave. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:4">88:4</a> I am counted with them that go down into the pit: I am as a man that hath no strength: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:5">88:5</a> Free among the dead, like the slain that lie in the grave, whom thou rememberest no more: and they are cut off from thy hand. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:6">88:6</a> Thou hast laid me in the lowest pit, in darkness, in the deeps. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:7">88:7</a> Thy wrath lieth hard upon me, and thou hast afflicted me with all thy waves. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:8">88:8</a> Thou hast put away my acquaintance far from me; thou hast made me an abomination to them: I am shut up, and I cannot come forth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:9">88:9</a> My eye mourneth by reason of affliction: LORD, I have called daily upon thee, I have stretched out my hands to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:10">88:10</a> Wilt thou show wonders to the dead? shall the dead arise and praise thee? Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:11">88:11</a> Shall thy loving-kindness be declared in the grave? or thy faithfulness in destruction? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:12">88:12</a> Shall thy wonders be known in the dark? and thy righteousness in the land of forgetfulness? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:13">88:13</a> But to thee have I cried, O LORD; and in the morning shall my prayer come before thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:14">88:14</a> LORD, why castest thou off my soul? why hidest thou thy face from me? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:15">88:15</a> I am afflicted and ready to die from my youth up: while I suffer thy terrors I am distracted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:16">88:16</a> Thy fierce wrath goeth over me; thy terrors have cut me off. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:17">88:17</a> They came around me daily like water; they encompassed me together. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:18">88:18</a> Lover and friend hast thou put far from me, and my acquaintance into darkness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:1">89:1</a> Maschil of Ethan the Ezrahite. I will sing of the mercies of the LORD for ever: with my mouth will I make known thy faithfulness to all generations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:2">89:2</a> For I have said, Mercy shall be built up for ever: thy faithfulness wilt thou establish in the very heavens. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:3">89:3</a> I have made a covenant with my chosen, I have sworn to David my servant, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:4">89:4</a> Thy seed will I establish for ever, and build up thy throne to all generations. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:5">89:5</a> And the heavens shall praise thy wonders, O LORD; thy faithfulness also in the congregation of the saints. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:6">89:6</a> For who in the heaven can be compared to the LORD? who among the sons of the mighty can be likened to the LORD? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:7">89:7</a> God is greatly to be feared in the assembly of the saints, and to be had in reverence by all them that are about him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:8">89:8</a> O LORD God of hosts, who is a strong LORD like to thee? or to thy faithfulness around thee? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:9">89:9</a> Thou rulest the raging of the sea: when its waves arise, thou stillest them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:10">89:10</a> Thou hast broken Rahab in pieces, as one that is slain; thou hast scattered thy enemies with thy strong arm. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:11">89:11</a> The heavens are thine, the earth also is thine: as for the world, and the fullness of it, thou hast founded them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:12">89:12</a> The north and the south thou hast created them: Tabor and Hermon shall rejoice in thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:13">89:13</a> Thou hast a mighty arm: strong is thy hand, and high is thy right hand. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:14">89:14</a> Justice and judgment are the habitation of thy throne: mercy and truth shall go before thy face. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:15">89:15</a> Blessed are the people that know the joyful sound: they shall walk, O LORD, in the light of thy countenance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:16">89:16</a> In thy name shall they rejoice all the day: and in thy righteousness shall they be exalted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:17">89:17</a> For thou art the glory of their strength: and in thy favor our horn shall be exalted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:18">89:18</a> For the LORD is our defense; and the Holy One of Israel is our king. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:19">89:19</a> Then thou didst speak in vision to thy holy one, and say, I have laid help upon one that is mighty; I have exalted one chosen out of the people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:20">89:20</a> I have found David my servant; with my holy oil have I anointed him: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:21">89:21</a> With whom my hand shall be established: my arm also shall strengthen him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:22">89:22</a> The enemy shall not exact upon him; nor the son of wickedness afflict him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:23">89:23</a> And I will beat down his foes before his face, and afflict them that hate him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:24">89:24</a> But my faithfulness and my mercy shall be with him: and in my name shall his horn be exalted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:25">89:25</a> I will set his hand also in the sea, and his right hand in the rivers. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:26">89:26</a> He shall cry to me, Thou art my father, my God, and the rock of my salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:27">89:27</a> Also I will make him my first-born, higher than the kings of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:28">89:28</a> My mercy will I keep for him for evermore, and my covenant shall stand fast with him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:29">89:29</a> His seed also will I make to endure for ever, and his throne as the days of heaven. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:30">89:30</a> If his children forsake my law, and walk not in my judgments; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:31">89:31</a> If they break my statutes, and keep not my commandments; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:32">89:32</a> Then will I visit their transgression with the rod, and their iniquity with stripes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:33">89:33</a> Nevertheless my loving-kindness will I not utterly take from him, nor suffer my faithfulness to fail. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:34">89:34</a> My covenant will I not break, nor alter the thing that hath gone out of my lips. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:35">89:35</a> Once have I sworn by my holiness that I will not lie to David. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:36">89:36</a> His seed shall endure for ever, and his throne as the sun before me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:37">89:37</a> It shall be established for ever as the moon, and as a faithful witness in heaven. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:38">89:38</a> But thou hast cast off and abhorred, thou hast been wroth with thy anointed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:39">89:39</a> Thou hast made void the covenant of thy servant: thou hast profaned his crown by casting it to the ground. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:40">89:40</a> Thou hast broken down all his hedges; thou hast brought his strong holds to ruin. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:41">89:41</a> All that pass by the way plunder him: he is a reproach to his neighbors. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:42">89:42</a> Thou hast set up the right hand of his adversaries; thou hast made all his enemies to rejoice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:43">89:43</a> Thou hast also turned the edge of his sword, and hast not made him to stand in the battle. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:44">89:44</a> Thou hast made his glory to cease, and cast his throne down to the ground. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:45">89:45</a> The days of his youth hast thou shortened: thou hast covered him with shame. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:46">89:46</a> How long, LORD, wilt thou hide thyself? for ever? shall thy wrath burn like fire? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:47">89:47</a> Remember how short my time is: why hast thou made all men in vain? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:48">89:48</a> What man is he that liveth, and shall not see death? shall he deliver his soul from the hand of the grave? Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:49">89:49</a> Lord, where are thy former loving-kindnesses, which thou didst swear to David in thy truth? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:50">89:50</a> Remember, Lord, the reproach of thy servants; how I do bear in my bosom the reproach of all the mighty people; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:51">89:51</a> With which thy enemies have reproached, O LORD; with which they have reproached the footsteps of thy anointed </p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:52">89:52</a> Blessed be the LORD for evermore. Amen and amen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:1">90:1</a> A prayer of Moses the man of God. Lord, thou hast been our dwelling-place in all generations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:2">90:2</a> Before the mountains were brought forth, or ever thou hadst formed the earth and the world, even from everlasting to everlasting, thou art God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:3">90:3</a> Thou turnest man to destruction; and sayest, Return, ye children of men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:4">90:4</a> For a thousand years in thy sight are but as yesterday when it is past, and as a watch in the night. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:5">90:5</a> Thou carriest them away as with a flood; they are as a sleep; in the morning they are like grass which groweth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:6">90:6</a> In the morning it flourisheth, and groweth; in the evening it is cut down, and withereth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:7">90:7</a> For we are consumed by thy anger, and by thy wrath are we troubled. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:8">90:8</a> Thou hast set our iniquities before thee, our secret sins in the light of thy countenance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:9">90:9</a> For all our days are passed away in thy wrath: we spend our years, as a tale that is told. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:10">90:10</a> The days of our years are seventy years; and if by reason of strength they are eighty years, yet is their strength labor and sorrow; for it is soon cut off, and we fly away. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:11">90:11</a> Who knoweth the power of thy anger? even according to thy fear, so is thy wrath. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:12">90:12</a> So teach us to number our days, that we may apply our hearts to wisdom. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:13">90:13</a> Return, O LORD, how long? and repent thou concerning thy servants. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:14">90:14</a> O satisfy us early with thy mercy; that we may rejoice and be glad all our days. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:15">90:15</a> Make us glad according to the days in which thou hast afflicted us, and the years in which we have seen evil. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:16">90:16</a> Let thy work appear to thy servants, and thy glory to their children. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:17">90:17</a> And let the beauty of the LORD our God be upon us: and establish thou the work of our hands upon us; yes, the work of our hands establish thou it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:1">91:1</a> He that dwelleth in the secret place of the Most High shall abide under the shadow of the Almighty. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:2">91:2</a> I will say of the LORD, He is my refuge and my fortress: my God; in him will I trust. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:3">91:3</a> Surely he shall deliver thee from the snare of the fowler, and from the noisome pestilence. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:4">91:4</a> He shall cover thee with his feathers, and under his wings shalt thou trust: his truth shall be thy shield and buckler. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:5">91:5</a> Thou shalt not be afraid for the terror by night; nor for the arrow that flieth by day; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:6">91:6</a> Nor for the pestilence that walketh in darkness; nor for the destruction that wasteth at noon-day. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:7">91:7</a> A thousand shall fall at thy side, and ten thousand at thy right hand; but it shall not come nigh thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:8">91:8</a> Only with thy eyes shalt thou behold and see the reward of the wicked. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:9">91:9</a> Because thou hast made the LORD who is my refuge, even the Most High, thy habitation; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:10">91:10</a> There shall no evil befall thee, neither shall any plague come nigh thy dwelling. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:11">91:11</a> For he shall give his angels charge over thee, to keep thee in all thy ways. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:12">91:12</a> They shall bear thee up in their hands, lest thou dash thy foot against a stone. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:13">91:13</a> Thou shalt tread upon the lion and adder: the young lion and the dragon shalt thou trample under feet. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:14">91:14</a> Because he hath set his love upon me, therefore will I deliver him: I will set him on high, because he hath known my name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:15">91:15</a> He shall call upon me, and I will answer him: I will be with him in trouble; I will deliver him, and honor him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:16">91:16</a> With long life will I satisfy him, and show him my salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:1">92:1</a> A Psalm or Song for the sabbath day. It is a good thing to give thanks to the LORD, and to sing praises to thy name, O Most High. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:2">92:2</a> To show forth thy loving-kindness in the morning, and thy faithfulness every night. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:3">92:3</a> Upon an instrument of ten strings, and upon the psaltery; upon the harp with a solemn sound. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:4">92:4</a> For thou, LORD, hast made me glad through thy work: I will triumph in the works of thy hands. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:5">92:5</a> O LORD, how great are thy works! and thy thoughts are very deep. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:6">92:6</a> A brutish man knoweth not; neither doth a fool understand this. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:7">92:7</a> When the wicked spring as the grass, and when all the workers of iniquity do flourish; it is that they shall be destroyed for ever: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:8">92:8</a> But thou, LORD, art most high for evermore. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:9">92:9</a> For lo, thy enemies, O LORD, for lo, thy enemies shall perish; all the workers of iniquity shall be scattered. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:10">92:10</a> But my horn shalt thou exalt like the horn of an unicorn: I shall be anointed with fresh oil. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:11">92:11</a> My eye also shall see my desire on my enemies, and my ears shall hear my desire of the wicked that rise up against me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:12">92:12</a> The righteous shall flourish like the palm-tree; he shall grow like a cedar in Lebanon. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:13">92:13</a> Those that are planted in the house of the LORD shall flourish in the courts of our God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:14">92:14</a> They shall still bring forth fruit in old age; they shall be fat and flourishing; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:15">92:15</a> To show that the LORD is upright: he is my rock, and there is no unrighteousness in him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:1">93:1</a> The LORD reigneth, he is clothed with majesty; the LORD is clothed with strength, with which he hath girded himself: the world also is established, that it cannot be moved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:2">93:2</a> Thy throne is established of old: thou art from everlasting. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:3">93:3</a> The floods have lifted up, O LORD, the floods have lifted up their voice; the floods lift their waves. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:4">93:4</a> The LORD on high is mightier than the noise of many waters, yes, than the mighty waves of the sea. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:5">93:5</a> Thy testimonies are very sure: holiness becometh thy house, O LORD, for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:1">94:1</a> O LORD God, to whom vengeance belongeth; O God, to whom vengeance belongeth, show thyself. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:2">94:2</a> Lift up thyself, thou judge of the earth: render a reward to the proud. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:3">94:3</a> LORD, how long shall the wicked, how long shall the wicked triumph? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:4">94:4</a> How long shall they utter and speak hard things? and all the workers of iniquity boast themselves? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:5">94:5</a> They break in pieces thy people, O LORD, and afflict thy heritage. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:6">94:6</a> They slay the widow and the stranger, and murder the fatherless. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:7">94:7</a> Yet they say, The LORD will not see, neither will the God of Jacob regard it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:8">94:8</a> Understand, ye brutish among the people: and ye fools, when will ye be wise? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:9">94:9</a> He that planted the ear, shall he not hear? he that formed the eye, shall he not see? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:10">94:10</a> He that chastiseth the heathen, shall he not correct? he that teacheth man knowledge, shall he not know? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:11">94:11</a> The LORD knoweth the thoughts of man, that they are vanity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:12">94:12</a> Blessed is the man whom thou chastenest, O LORD, and teachest him out of thy law; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:13">94:13</a> That thou mayest give him rest from the days of adversity, until the pit be digged for the wicked. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:14">94:14</a> For the LORD will not cast off his people, neither will he forsake his inheritance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:15">94:15</a> But judgment shall return to righteousness: and all the upright in heart shall follow it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:16">94:16</a> Who will rise up for me against the evil-doers? or who will stand up for me against the workers of iniquity? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:17">94:17</a> Unless the LORD had been my help, my soul had almost dwelt in silence. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:18">94:18</a> When I said, My foot slippeth; thy mercy, O LORD, held me up. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:19">94:19</a> In the multitude of my thoughts within me, thy comforts delight my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:20">94:20</a> Shall the throne of iniquity have fellowship with thee, which frameth mischief by a law? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:21">94:21</a> They assemble themselves against the soul of the righteous, and condemn the innocent blood. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:22">94:22</a> But the LORD is my defense; and my God is the rock of my refuge. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:23">94:23</a> And he will bring upon them their own iniquity, and will cut them off in their own wickedness; yes, the LORD our God will cut them off. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:1">95:1</a> O come, let us sing to the LORD: let us make a joyful noise to the rock of our salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:2">95:2</a> Let us come before his presence with thanksgiving, and make a joyful noise to him with psalms. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:3">95:3</a> For the LORD is a great God, and a great King above all gods. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:4">95:4</a> In his hand are the deep places of the earth: the strength of the hills is his also. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:5">95:5</a> The sea is his, and he made it: and his hands formed the dry land. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:6">95:6</a> O come, let us worship and bow down: let us kneel before the LORD our maker. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:7">95:7</a> For he is our God; and we are the people of his pasture, and the sheep of his hand. To-day, if ye will hear his voice, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:8">95:8</a> Harden not your heart, as in the provocation, and as in the day of temptation in the wilderness: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:9">95:9</a> When your fathers tempted me, proved me, and saw my work. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:10">95:10</a> Forty years long was I grieved with this generation, and said, It is a people that do err in their heart, and they have not known my ways: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:11">95:11</a> To whom I swore in my wrath, that they should not enter into my rest. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:1">96:1</a> O sing to the LORD a new song: sing to the LORD, all the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:2">96:2</a> Sing to the LORD, bless his name; show forth his salvation from day to day. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:3">96:3</a> Declare his glory among the heathen, his wonders among all people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:4">96:4</a> For the LORD is great, and greatly to be praised: he is to be feared above all gods. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:5">96:5</a> For all the gods of the nations are idols: but the LORD made the heavens. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:6">96:6</a> Honor and majesty are before him: strength and beauty are in his sanctuary. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:7">96:7</a> Give to the LORD, O ye kindreds of the people, give to the LORD glory and strength. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:8">96:8</a> Give to the LORD the glory due to his name: bring an offering, and come into his courts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:9">96:9</a> O worship the LORD in the beauty of holiness: fear before him, all the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:10">96:10</a> Say among the heathen that the LORD reigneth: the world also shall be established that it shall not be moved: he will judge the people righteously. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:11">96:11</a> Let the heavens rejoice, and let the earth be glad; let the sea roar, and the fullness of it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:12">96:12</a> Let the field be joyful, and all that is in it: then shall all the trees of the wood rejoice before the LORD: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:13">96:13</a> For he cometh, for he cometh to judge the earth: he will judge the world with righteousness, and the people with his truth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:1">97:1</a> The LORD reigneth; let the earth rejoice; let the multitude of isles be glad. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:2">97:2</a> Clouds and darkness surround him: righteousness and judgment are the habitation of his throne. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:3">97:3</a> A fire goeth before him, and burneth up his enemies round about. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:4">97:4</a> His lightnings enlightened the world: the earth saw, and trembled. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:5">97:5</a> The hills melted like wax at the presence of the LORD, at the presence of the Lord of the whole earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:6">97:6</a> The heavens declare his righteousness, and all the people see his glory. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:7">97:7</a> Confounded be all they that serve graven images, that boast themselves of idols; worship him, all ye gods. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:8">97:8</a> Zion heard, and was glad; and the daughters of Judah rejoiced because of thy judgments, O LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:9">97:9</a> For thou, LORD, art high above all the earth: thou art exalted far above all gods. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:10">97:10</a> Ye that love the LORD, hate evil: he preserveth the souls of his saints; he delivereth them out of the hand of the wicked. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:11">97:11</a> Light is sown for the righteous, and gladness for the upright in heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:12">97:12</a> Rejoice in the LORD, ye righteous; and give thanks at the remembrance of his holiness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:1">98:1</a> A Psalm. O sing to the LORD a new song; for he hath done marvelous things: his right hand, and his holy arm, hath gotten him the victory. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:2">98:2</a> The LORD hath made known his salvation: his righteousness hath he openly shown in the sight of the heathen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:3">98:3</a> He hath remembered his mercy and his truth towards the house of Israel: all the ends of the earth have seen the salvation of our God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:4">98:4</a> Make a joyful noise to the LORD, all the earth: make a loud noise, and rejoice, and sing praise. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:5">98:5</a> Sing to the LORD with the harp; with the harp, and the voice of a psalm. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:6">98:6</a> With trumpets and sound of cornet make a joyful noise before the LORD, the King. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:7">98:7</a> Let the sea roar, and the fullness of it, the world, and they that dwell therein. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:8">98:8</a> Let the floods clap their hands: let the hills be joyful together </p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:9">98:9</a> Before the LORD; for he cometh to judge the earth: with righteousness will he judge the world, and the people with equity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:1">99:1</a> The LORD reigneth; let the people tremble: he setteth between the cherubim; let the earth be moved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:2">99:2</a> The LORD is great in Zion; and he is high above all people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:3">99:3</a> Let them praise thy great and terrible name; for it is holy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:4">99:4</a> The king's strength also loveth judgment; thou dost establish equity, thou executest judgment and righteousness in Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:5">99:5</a> Exalt ye the LORD our God, and worship at his footstool; for he is holy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:6">99:6</a> Moses and Aaron among his priests, and Samuel among them that call upon his name; they called upon the LORD, and he answered them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:7">99:7</a> He spoke to them in the cloudy pillar: they kept his testimonies, and the ordinance that he gave them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:8">99:8</a> Thou didst answer them, O LORD our God: thou wast a God that forgavest them, though thou tookest vengeance of their inventions. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:9">99:9</a> Exalt the LORD our God, and worship at his holy hill; for the LORD our God is holy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:1">100:1</a> A Psalm of praise. Make a joyful noise to the LORD, all ye lands. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:2">100:2</a> Serve the LORD with gladness: come before his presence with singing. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:3">100:3</a> Know ye that the LORD he is God: it is he that hath made us, and not we ourselves; we are his people, and the sheep of his pasture. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:4">100:4</a> Enter into his gates with thanksgiving, and into his courts with praise: be thankful to him, and bless his name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:5">100:5</a> For the LORD is good; his mercy is everlasting; and his truth endureth to all generations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:1">101:1</a> A Psalm of David. I will sing of mercy and judgment: to thee, O LORD, will I sing. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:2">101:2</a> I will behave myself wisely in a perfect way. O when wilt thou come to me? I will walk within my house with a perfect heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:3">101:3</a> I will set no wicked thing before my eyes: I hate the work of them that turn aside; it shall not cleave to me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:4">101:4</a> A froward heart shall depart from me: I will not know a wicked person. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:5">101:5</a> Whoever privily slandereth his neighbor, him will I cut off: him that hath a high look and a proud heart I will not suffer. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:6">101:6</a> My eyes shall be upon the faithful of the land, that they may dwell with me: he that walketh in a perfect way, he shall serve me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:7">101:7</a> He that worketh deceit shall not dwell within my house: he that telleth lies shall not tarry in my sight. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:8">101:8</a> I will early destroy all the wicked of the land; that I may cut off all who practice wickedness from the city of the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:1">102:1</a> A Prayer of the afflicted, when he is overwhelmed, and poureth out his complaint before the LORD. Hear my prayer, O LORD, and let my cry come to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:2">102:2</a> Hide not thy face from me in the day when I am in trouble; incline thy ear to me: in the day when I call, answer me speedily. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:3">102:3</a> For my days are consumed like smoke, and my bones are burned as an hearth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:4">102:4</a> My heart is smitten, and withered like grass; so that I forget to eat my bread. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:5">102:5</a> By reason of the voice of my groaning, my bones cleave to my skin. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:6">102:6</a> I am like a pelican of the wilderness: I am like an owl of the desert. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:7">102:7</a> I watch, and am as a sparrow alone upon the house top. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:8">102:8</a> My enemies reproach me all the day; and they that are enraged against me are sworn against me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:9">102:9</a> For I have eaten ashes like bread, and mingled my drink with weeping, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:10">102:10</a> Because of thy indignation and thy wrath: for thou hast lifted me up, and cast me down. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:11">102:11</a> My days are like a shadow that declineth; and I am withered like grass. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:12">102:12</a> But thou, O LORD, shalt endure for ever; and thy remembrance to all generations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:13">102:13</a> Thou shalt arise, and have mercy upon Zion: for the time to favor her, yes, the set time, is come. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:14">102:14</a> For thy servants take pleasure in her stones, and favor the dust thereof. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:15">102:15</a> So the heathen shall fear the name of the LORD: and all the kings of the earth thy glory. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:16">102:16</a> When the LORD shall build up Zion, he will appear in his glory. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:17">102:17</a> He will regard the prayer of the destitute, and not despise their prayer. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:18">102:18</a> This shall be written for the generation to come: and the people which shall be created shall praise the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:19">102:19</a> For he hath looked down from the hight of his sanctuary; from heaven hath the LORD beheld the earth; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:20">102:20</a> To hear the groaning of the prisoner; to loose those that are appointed to death; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:21">102:21</a> To declare the name of the LORD in Zion, and his praise in Jerusalem; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:22">102:22</a> When the people are assembled, and the kingdoms, to serve the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:23">102:23</a> He weakened my strength in the way; he shortened my days. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:24">102:24</a> I said, O my God, take me not away in the midst of my days: thy years are throughout all generations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:25">102:25</a> Of old hast thou laid the foundation of the earth: and the heavens are the work of thy hands. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:26">102:26</a> They shall perish, but thou wilt endure: yes, all of them shall grow old like a garment; as a vesture wilt thou change them, and they shall be changed: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:27">102:27</a> But thou art the same, and thy years will have no end. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:28">102:28</a> The children of thy servants shall continue, and their seed shall be established before thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:1">103:1</a> A Psalm of David. Bless the LORD, O my soul: and all that is within me, bless his holy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:2">103:2</a> Bless the LORD, O my soul, and forget not all his benefits: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:3">103:3</a> Who forgiveth all thy iniquities; who healeth all thy diseases; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:4">103:4</a> Who redeemeth thy life from destruction; who crowneth thee with loving-kindness and tender mercies; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:5">103:5</a> Who satisfieth thy mouth with good things; so that thy youth is renewed like the eagle's. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:6">103:6</a> The LORD executeth righteousness and judgment for all that are oppressed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:7">103:7</a> He made known his ways to Moses, his acts to the children of Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:8">103:8</a> The LORD is merciful and gracious, slow to anger, and abundant in mercy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:9">103:9</a> He will not always chide: neither will he keep his anger for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:10">103:10</a> He hath not dealt with us according to our sins; nor rewarded us according to our iniquities. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:11">103:11</a> For as the heaven is high above the earth, so great is his mercy towards them that fear him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:12">103:12</a> As far as the east is from the west, so far hath he removed our transgressions from us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:13">103:13</a> Like as a father pitieth his children, so the LORD pitieth them that fear him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:14">103:14</a> For he knoweth our frame; he remembereth that we are dust. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:15">103:15</a> As for man, his days are as grass: as a flower of the field, so he flourisheth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:16">103:16</a> For the wind passeth over it, and it is gone; and its place shall know it no more. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:17">103:17</a> But the mercy of the LORD is from everlasting to everlasting upon them that fear him, and his righteousness to children's children; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:18">103:18</a> To such as keep his covenant, and to those that remember his commandments to do them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:19">103:19</a> The LORD hath prepared his throne in the heavens; and his kingdom ruleth over all. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:20">103:20</a> Bless the LORD, ye his angels, that excel in strength, that do his commandments, hearkening to the voice of his word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:21">103:21</a> Bless ye the LORD, all ye his hosts; ye ministers of his, that do his pleasure. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:22">103:22</a> Bless the LORD, all his works in all places of his dominion: bless the LORD, O my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:1">104:1</a> Bless the LORD, O my soul. O LORD my God, thou art very great; thou art clothed with honor and majesty. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:2">104:2</a> Who coverest thyself with light as with a garment: who stretchest out the heavens like a curtain: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:3">104:3</a> Who layeth the beams of his chambers in the waters: who maketh the clouds his chariot: who walketh upon the wings of the wind: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:4">104:4</a> Who maketh his angels spirits; his ministers a flaming fire: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:5">104:5</a> Who laid the foundations of the earth, that it should not be removed for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:6">104:6</a> Thou coveredst it with the deep as with a garment: the waters stood above the mountains. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:7">104:7</a> At thy rebuke they fled; at the voice of thy thunder they hasted away. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:8">104:8</a> They go up by the mountains; they go down by the valleys to the place which thou hast founded for them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:9">104:9</a> Thou hast set a bound that they may not pass over; that they turn not again to cover the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:10">104:10</a> He sendeth the springs into the valleys, which run among the hills. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:11">104:11</a> They give drink to every beast of the field: the wild asses quench their thirst. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:12">104:12</a> By them shall the fowls of the heaven have their habitation, which sing among the branches. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:13">104:13</a> He watereth the hills from his chambers: the earth is satisfied with the fruit of thy works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:14">104:14</a> He causeth the grass to grow for the cattle, and herb for the service of man: that he may bring forth food out of the earth; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:15">104:15</a> And wine that maketh glad the heart of man, and oil to make his face to shine, and bread which strengtheneth man's heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:16">104:16</a> The trees of the LORD are full of sap; the cedars of Lebanon, which he hath planted; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:17">104:17</a> Where the birds make their nests: as for the stork, the fir-trees are her house. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:18">104:18</a> The high hills are a refuge for the wild goats; and the rocks for the conies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:19">104:19</a> He appointeth the moon for seasons: the sun knoweth his going down. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:20">104:20</a> Thou makest darkness, and it is night: in which all the beasts of the forest do creep forth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:21">104:21</a> The young lions roar after their prey, and seek their food from God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:22">104:22</a> The sun ariseth, they collect, and lay themselves down in their dens. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:23">104:23</a> Man goeth forth to his work and to his labor until the evening. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:24">104:24</a> O LORD, how manifold are thy works! in wisdom hast thou made them all: the earth is full of thy riches. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:25">104:25</a> So is this great and wide sea, in which are creeping animals innumerable, both small and great beasts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:26">104:26</a> There go the ships: there is that leviathan, which thou hast made to play therein. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:27">104:27</a> These wait all upon thee; that thou mayest give them their food in due season. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:28">104:28</a> That which thou givest them, they gather: thou openest thy hand, they are filled with good. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:29">104:29</a> Thou hidest thy face, they are troubled: thou takest away their breath, they die, and return to their dust. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:30">104:30</a> Thou sendest forth thy spirit, they are created: and thou renewest the face of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:31">104:31</a> The glory of the LORD shall endure for ever: the LORD shall rejoice in his works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:32">104:32</a> He looketh on the earth, and it trembleth: he toucheth the hills, and they smoke. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:33">104:33</a> I will sing to the LORD as long as I live: I will sing praise to my God while I have my being. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:34">104:34</a> My meditation of him shall be sweet: I will be glad in the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:35">104:35</a> Let sinners be consumed out of the earth, and let the wicked be no more. Bless thou the LORD, O my soul. Praise ye the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:1">105:1</a> O give thanks to the LORD; call upon his name: make known his deeds among the people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:2">105:2</a> Sing to him, sing psalms to him: talk ye of all his wondrous works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:3">105:3</a> Glory ye in his holy name: let the heart of them rejoice that seek the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:4">105:4</a> Seek the LORD, and his strength: seek his face evermore. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:5">105:5</a> Remember his wonderful works that he hath done; his wonders, and the judgments of his mouth; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:6">105:6</a> O ye seed of Abraham his servant, ye children of Jacob his chosen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:7">105:7</a> He is the LORD our God: his judgments are in all the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:8">105:8</a> He hath remembered his covenant for ever, the word which he commanded to a thousand generations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:9">105:9</a> Which covenant he made with Abraham, and his oath to Isaac; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:10">105:10</a> And confirmed the same to Jacob for a law, and to Israel for an everlasting covenant: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:11">105:11</a> Saying, To thee will I give the land of Canaan, the lot of your inheritance: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:12">105:12</a> When they were a few men in number; yes, very few, and strangers in it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:13">105:13</a> When they went from one nation to another, from one kingdom to another people; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:14">105:14</a> He suffered no man to do them wrong: yes, he reproved kings for their sakes; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:15">105:15</a> Saying, Touch not my anointed, and do my prophets no harm. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:16">105:16</a> Moreover he called for a famine upon the land: he broke the whole staff of bread. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:17">105:17</a> He sent a man before them, even Joseph, who was sold for a servant: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:18">105:18</a> Whose feet they hurt with fetters: he was laid in iron: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:19">105:19</a> Until the time that his word came: the word of the LORD tried him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:20">105:20</a> The king sent and loosed him; even the ruler of the people, and let him go free. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:21">105:21</a> He made him lord of his house, and ruler of all his substance: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:22">105:22</a> To bind his princes at his pleasure; and teach his senators wisdom. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:23">105:23</a> Israel also came into Egypt; and Jacob sojourned in the land of Ham. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:24">105:24</a> And he increased his people greatly; and made them stronger than their enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:25">105:25</a> He turned their heart to hate his people, to deal subtilly with his servants. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:26">105:26</a> He sent Moses his servant; and Aaron whom he had chosen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:27">105:27</a> They showed his signs among them, and wonders in the land of Ham. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:28">105:28</a> He sent darkness, and made it dark; and they rebelled not against his word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:29">105:29</a> He turned their waters into blood, and slew their fish. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:30">105:30</a> Their land brought forth frogs in abundance, in the chambers of their kings. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:31">105:31</a> He spoke, and there came divers sorts of flies, and lice in all their borders. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:32">105:32</a> He gave them hail for rain, and flaming fire in their land. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:33">105:33</a> He smote their vines also and their fig-trees; and broke the trees of their borders. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:34">105:34</a> He spoke, and the locusts came, and caterpillars, and that without number, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:35">105:35</a> And ate up all the herbs in their land, and devoured the fruit of their ground. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:36">105:36</a> He smote also all the first-born in their land, the chief of all their strength. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:37">105:37</a> He brought them forth also with silver and gold: and there was not one feeble person among their tribes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:38">105:38</a> Egypt was glad when they departed: for the fear of them fell upon them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:39">105:39</a> He spread a cloud for a covering; and fire to give light in the night. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:40">105:40</a> The people asked, and he brought quails, and satisfied them with the bread of heaven. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:41">105:41</a> He opened the rock, and the waters gushed out; they ran in the dry places like a river. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:42">105:42</a> For he remembered his holy promise, and Abraham his servant. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:43">105:43</a> And he brought forth his people with joy, and his chosen with gladness: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:44">105:44</a> And gave them the lands of the heathen: and they inherited the labor of the people; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:45">105:45</a> That they might observe his statutes, and keep his laws. Praise ye the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:1">106:1</a> Praise ye the LORD. O give thanks to the LORD; for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:2">106:2</a> Who can utter the mighty acts of the LORD? who can show forth all his praise? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:3">106:3</a> Blessed are they that keep judgment, and he that doeth righteousness at all times. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:4">106:4</a> Remember me, O LORD, with the favor that thou bearest to thy people: O visit me with thy salvation; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:5">106:5</a> That I may see the good of thy chosen, that I may rejoice in the gladness of thy nation, that I may glory with thy inheritance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:6">106:6</a> We have sinned with our fathers, we have committed iniquity, we have done wickedly. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:7">106:7</a> Our fathers understood not thy wonders in Egypt; they remembered not the multitude of thy mercies; but provoked him at the sea, even at the Red sea. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:8">106:8</a> Nevertheless he saved them for his name's sake, that he might make his mighty power to be known. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:9">106:9</a> He rebuked the Red sea also, and it was dried up: so he led them through the depths, as through the wilderness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:10">106:10</a> And he saved them from the hand of him that hated them, and redeemed them from the hand of the enemy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:11">106:11</a> And the waters covered their enemies: there was not one of them left. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:12">106:12</a> Then they believed his words; they sang his praise. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:13">106:13</a> They soon forgot his works; they waited not for his counsel: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:14">106:14</a> But lusted exceedingly in the wilderness, and tempted God in the desert. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:15">106:15</a> And he gave them their request; but sent leanness into their soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:16">106:16</a> They envied Moses also in the camp, and Aaron the saint of the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:17">106:17</a> The earth opened and swallowed up Dathan, and covered the company of Abiram. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:18">106:18</a> And a fire was kindled in their company; the flame burned up the wicked. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:19">106:19</a> They made a calf in Horeb, and worshiped the molten image. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:20">106:20</a> Thus they changed their glory into the similitude of an ox that eateth grass. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:21">106:21</a> They forgot God their savior, who had done great things in Egypt; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:22">106:22</a> Wondrous works in the land of Ham, and terrible things by the Red sea. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:23">106:23</a> Therefore he said that he would destroy them, had not Moses his chosen stood before him in the breach, to turn away his wrath, lest he should destroy them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:24">106:24</a> Yes, they despised the pleasant land, they believed not his word: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:25">106:25</a> But murmured in their tents, and hearkened not to the voice of the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:26">106:26</a> Therefore he lifted up his hand against them, to overthrow them in the wilderness: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:27">106:27</a> To overthrow their seed also among the nations, and to scatter them in the lands. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:28">106:28</a> They joined themselves also to Baal-peor, and ate the sacrifices of the dead. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:29">106:29</a> Thus they provoked him to anger with their inventions: and the plague broke in upon them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:30">106:30</a> Then stood up Phinehas, and executed judgment: and so the plague was stayed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:31">106:31</a> And that was counted to him for righteousness to all generations for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:32">106:32</a> They angered him also at the waters of strife, so that it went ill with Moses for their sakes: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:33">106:33</a> Because they provoked his spirit, so that he spoke unadvisedly with his lips. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:34">106:34</a> They did not destroy the nations, concerning whom the LORD commanded them: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:35">106:35</a> But were mingled among the heathen, and learned their works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:36">106:36</a> And they served their idols: which were a snare to them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:37">106:37</a> Yes, they sacrificed their sons and their daughters to demons, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:38">106:38</a> And shed innocent blood, even the blood of their sons and of their daughters, whom they sacrificed to the idols of Canaan: and the land was polluted with blood. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:39">106:39</a> Thus were they defiled with their own works, and went astray with their own inventions. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:40">106:40</a> Therefore was the wrath of the LORD kindled against his people, insomuch that he abhorred his own inheritance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:41">106:41</a> And he gave them into the hand of the heathen; and they that hated them ruled over them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:42">106:42</a> Their enemies also oppressed them, and they were brought into subjection under their hand. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:43">106:43</a> Many times did he deliver them; but they provoked him with their counsel; and were brought low for their iniquity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:44">106:44</a> Nevertheless he regarded their affliction, when he heard their cry: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:45">106:45</a> And he remembered for them his covenant, and repented according to the multitude of his mercies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:46">106:46</a> He made them also to be pitied by all those that carried them captives. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:47">106:47</a> Save us, O LORD our God, and gather us from among the heathen, to give thanks to thy holy name, and to triumph in thy praise. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:48">106:48</a> Blessed be the LORD God of Israel from everlasting to everlasting: and let all the people say, Amen. Praise ye the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:1">107:1</a> O give thanks to the LORD, for he is good; for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:2">107:2</a> Let the redeemed of the LORD say so, whom he hath redeemed from the hand of the enemy; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:3">107:3</a> And gathered them out of the lands, from the east, and from the west, from the north, and from the south. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:4">107:4</a> They wandered in the wilderness in a solitary way; they found no city to dwell in. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:5">107:5</a> Hungry and thirsty, their soul fainted in them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:6">107:6</a> Then they cried to the LORD in their trouble, and he delivered them out of their distresses. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:7">107:7</a> And he led them forth by the right way, that they might go to a city of habitation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:8">107:8</a> Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, and for his wonderful works to the children of men! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:9">107:9</a> For he satisfieth the longing soul, and filleth the hungry soul with goodness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:10">107:10</a> Such as sit in darkness and in the shades of death, being bound in affliction and iron; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:11">107:11</a> Because they rebelled against the words of God, and contemned the counsel of the Most High: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:12">107:12</a> Therefore he brought down their heart with labor; they fell down, and there was none to help. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:13">107:13</a> Then they cried to the LORD in their trouble, and he saved them out of their distresses. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:14">107:14</a> He brought them out of darkness and the shades of death, and broke their bands asunder. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:15">107:15</a> Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, and for his wonderful works to the children of men! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:16">107:16</a> For he hath broken the gates of brass, and cut the bars of iron asunder. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:17">107:17</a> Fools, because of their transgression, and because of their iniquities, are afflicted. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:18">107:18</a> Their soul abhorreth all manner of food; and they draw near to the gates of death. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:19">107:19</a> Then they cry to the LORD in their trouble, he saveth them out of their distresses. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:20">107:20</a> He sent his word, and healed them, and delivered them from their destructions. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:21">107:21</a> Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, and for his wonderful works to the children of men! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:22">107:22</a> And let them sacrifice the sacrifices of thanksgiving, and declare his works with rejoicing. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:23">107:23</a> They that go down to the sea in ships, that do business on great waters; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:24">107:24</a> These see the works of the LORD, and his wonders in the deep. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:25">107:25</a> For he commandeth, and raiseth the stormy wind, which lifteth up its waves. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:26">107:26</a> They mount up to the heaven, they go down again to the depths: their soul is melted because of trouble. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:27">107:27</a> They reel to and fro, and stagger like a drunken man, and are at their wit's end. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:28">107:28</a> Then they cry to the LORD in their trouble, and he bringeth them out of their distresses. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:29">107:29</a> He maketh the storm a calm, so that the waves of the sea are still. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:30">107:30</a> Then are they glad because they are quiet; so he bringeth them to their desired haven. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:31">107:31</a> Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, and for his wonderful works to the children of men! </p>
