 <p><a name="an_107:32">107:32</a> Let them exalt him also in the congregation of the people, and praise him in the assembly of the elders. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:33">107:33</a> He turneth rivers into a wilderness, and the water-springs into dry ground; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:34">107:34</a> A fruitful land into barrenness, for the wickedness of them that dwell in it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:35">107:35</a> He turneth the wilderness into a standing water, and dry ground into water-springs. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:36">107:36</a> And there he maketh the hungry to dwell, that they may prepare a city for habitation; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:37">107:37</a> And sow the fields, and plant vineyards, which may yield fruits of increase. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:38">107:38</a> He blesseth them also, so that they are multiplied greatly; and suffereth not their cattle to decrease. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:39">107:39</a> Again, they are diminished and brought low through oppression, affliction, and sorrow. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:40">107:40</a> He poureth contempt upon princes, and causeth them to wander in the wilderness, where there is no way. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:41">107:41</a> Yet he setteth the poor on high from affliction, and maketh him families like a flock. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:42">107:42</a> The righteous shall see it, and rejoice: and all iniquity shall stop her mouth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:43">107:43</a> Whoever is wise, and will observe these things, even they shall understand the loving-kindness of the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:1">108:1</a> A Song or Psalm of David. O God, my heart is fixed; I will sing and give praise, even with my glory. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:2">108:2</a> Awake, psaltery and harp: I myself will awake early. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:3">108:3</a> I will praise thee, O LORD, among the people: and I will sing praises to thee among the nations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:4">108:4</a> For thy mercy is great above the heavens: and thy truth reacheth to the clouds. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:5">108:5</a> Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens: and thy glory above all the earth; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:6">108:6</a> That thy beloved may be delivered: save with thy right hand, and answer me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:7">108:7</a> God hath spoken in his holiness; I will rejoice, I will divide Shechem, and measure out the valley of Succoth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:8">108:8</a> Gilead is mine; Manasseh is mine; Ephraim also is the strength of my head; Judah is my lawgiver; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:9">108:9</a> Moab is my washpot; over Edom will I cast out my shoe; over Philistia will I triumph. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:10">108:10</a> Who will bring me into the strong city: who will lead me into Edom? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:11">108:11</a> Wilt not thou, O God, who hast cast us off? and wilt not thou, O God, go forth with our armies? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:12">108:12</a> Give us help from trouble: for vain is the help of man. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:13">108:13</a> Through God we shall do valiantly: for he will tread down our enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:1">109:1</a> To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David. Hold not thy peace, O God of my praise; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:2">109:2</a> For the mouth of the wicked and the mouth of the deceitful are opened against me: they have spoken against me with a lying tongue. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:3">109:3</a> They encompassed me also with words of hatred; and fought against me without a cause. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:4">109:4</a> For my love they are my adversaries: but I give myself to prayer. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:5">109:5</a> And they have rewarded me evil for good, and hatred for my love. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:6">109:6</a> Set thou a wicked man over him: and let Satan stand at his right hand. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:7">109:7</a> When he shall be judged, let him be condemned: and let his prayer become sin. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:8">109:8</a> Let his days be few; and let another take his office. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:9">109:9</a> Let his children be fatherless, and his wife a widow. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:10">109:10</a> Let his children be continually vagabonds, and beg: let them seek their bread also out of their desolate places. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:11">109:11</a> Let the extortioner catch all that he hath; and let strangers spoil his labor. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:12">109:12</a> Let there be none to extend mercy to him: neither let there be any to favor his fatherless children. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:13">109:13</a> Let his posterity be cut off; and in the generation following let their name be blotted out. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:14">109:14</a> Let the iniquity of his fathers be remembered with the LORD; and let not the sin of his mother be blotted out. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:15">109:15</a> Let them be before the LORD continually, that he may cut off the memory of them from the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:16">109:16</a> Because that he remembered not to show mercy, but persecuted the poor and needy man, that he might even slay the broken in heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:17">109:17</a> As he loved cursing, so let it come to him: as he delighted not in blessing, so let it be far from him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:18">109:18</a> As he clothed himself with cursing like as with his garment, so let it come into his bowels like water, and like oil into his bones. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:19">109:19</a> Let it be to him as the garment which covereth him, and for a girdle with which he is girded continually. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:20">109:20</a> Let this be the reward of my adversaries from the LORD, and of them that speak evil against my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:21">109:21</a> But do thou for me, O GOD the Lord, for thy name's sake: because thy mercy is good, deliver thou me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:22">109:22</a> For I am poor and needy, and my heart is wounded within me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:23">109:23</a> I am gone like the shadow when it declineth: I am tossed up and down as the locust. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:24">109:24</a> My knees are weak through fasting; and my flesh faileth of fatness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:25">109:25</a> I became also a reproach to them: when they looked upon me they shook their heads. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:26">109:26</a> Help me, O LORD my God: O save me according to thy mercy: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:27">109:27</a> That they may know that this is thy hand; that thou, LORD, hast done it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:28">109:28</a> Let them curse, but bless thou: when they arise, let them be ashamed; but let thy servant rejoice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:29">109:29</a> Let my adversaries be clothed with shame, and let them cover themselves with their own confusion, as with a mantle. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:30">109:30</a> I will greatly praise the LORD with my mouth; yes, I will praise him among the multitude. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:31">109:31</a> For he will stand at the right hand of the poor, to save him from those that condemn his soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:1">110:1</a> A Psalm of David. The LORD said to my Lord, Sit thou at my right hand, until I make thy enemies thy footstool. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:2">110:2</a> The LORD will send the rod of thy strength out of Zion: rule thou in the midst of thy enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:3">110:3</a> Thy people shall be willing in the day of thy power, in the beauties of holiness: from the womb of the morning, thou hast the dew of thy youth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:4">110:4</a> The LORD hath sworn, and will not repent, Thou art a priest for ever after the order of Melchisedek. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:5">110:5</a> The Lord at thy right hand will strike through kings in the day of his wrath. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:6">110:6</a> He will judge among the heathen, he will fill the places with the dead bodies; he will wound the heads over many countries. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:7">110:7</a> He will drink of the brook in the way: therefore will he lift up the head. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:1">111:1</a> Praise ye the LORD. I will praise the LORD with my whole heart, in the assembly of the upright, and in the congregation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:2">111:2</a> The works of the LORD are great, sought out by all them that have pleasure in them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:3">111:3</a> His work is honorable and glorious: and his righteousness endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:4">111:4</a> He hath made his wonderful works to be remembered: the LORD is gracious and full of compassion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:5">111:5</a> He hath given food to them that fear him: he will ever be mindful of his covenant. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:6">111:6</a> He hath shown his people the power of his works, that he may give them the heritage of the heathen. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:7">111:7</a> The works of his hands are verity and judgment; all his commandments are sure. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:8">111:8</a> They stand fast for ever and ever, and are done in truth and uprightness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:9">111:9</a> He sent redemption to his people: he hath commanded his covenant for ever: holy and reverend is his name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:10">111:10</a> The fear of the LORD is the beginning of wisdom: a good understanding have all they that do his commandments: his praise endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:1">112:1</a> Praise ye the LORD. Blessed is the man that feareth the LORD, that delighteth greatly in his commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:2">112:2</a> His seed shall be mighty upon earth: the generation of the upright shall be blessed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:3">112:3</a> Wealth and riches shall be in his house: and his righteousness endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:4">112:4</a> To the upright there ariseth light in darkness: he is gracious, and full of compassion, and righteous. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:5">112:5</a> A good man showeth favor, and lendeth: he will guide his affairs with discretion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:6">112:6</a> Surely he shall not be moved for ever: the righteous shall be in everlasting remembrance. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:7">112:7</a> He shall not be afraid of evil tidings: his heart is fixed, trusting in the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:8">112:8</a> His heart is established, he shall not be afraid, until he seeth his desire upon his enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:9">112:9</a> He hath dispersed, he hath given to the poor; his righteousness endureth for ever; his horn shall be exalted with honor. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:10">112:10</a> The wicked shall see it, and be grieved; he shall gnash with his teeth, and melt away: the desire of the wicked shall perish. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:1">113:1</a> Praise ye the LORD. Praise, O ye servants of the LORD, praise the name of the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:2">113:2</a> Blessed be the name of the LORD from this time forth and for evermore. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:3">113:3</a> From the rising of the sun to the going down of the same the LORD'S name is to be praised. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:4">113:4</a> The LORD is high above all nations, and his glory above the heavens. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:5">113:5</a> Who is like to the LORD our God, who dwelleth on high. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:6">113:6</a> Who humbleth himself to behold the things that are in heaven, and in the earth! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:7">113:7</a> He raiseth the poor out of the dust, and lifteth the needy out of the dunghill; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:8">113:8</a> That he may set him with princes, even with the princes of his people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:9">113:9</a> He maketh the barren woman to keep house, and to be a joyful mother of children. Praise ye the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:1">114:1</a> When Israel went out of Egypt, the house of Jacob from a people of a foreign language; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:2">114:2</a> Judah was his sanctuary, and Israel his dominion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:3">114:3</a> The sea saw it, and fled: Jordan was driven back. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:4">114:4</a> The mountains skipped like rams, and the little hills like lambs. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:5">114:5</a> What ailed thee, O thou sea, that thou fleddest? thou Jordan, that thou wast driven back? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:6">114:6</a> Ye mountains, that ye skipped like rams; and ye little hills, like lambs? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:7">114:7</a> Tremble, thou earth, at the presence of the Lord, at the presence of the God of Jacob; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:8">114:8</a> Who turned the rock into a standing water, the flint into a fountain of waters. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:1">115:1</a> Not to us, O LORD, not to us, but to thy name give glory, for thy mercy, and for thy truth's sake. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:2">115:2</a> Why should the heathen say, Where is now their God? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:3">115:3</a> But our God is in the heavens: he hath done whatever he pleased. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:4">115:4</a> Their idols are silver and gold; the work of men's hands. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:5">115:5</a> They have mouths, but they speak not: eyes have they, but they see not: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:6">115:6</a> They have ears, but they hear not: noses have they, but they smell not: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:7">115:7</a> They have hands, but they handle not: feet have they, but they walk not: neither speak they through their throat. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:8">115:8</a> They that make them are like them; so is every one that trusteth in them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:9">115:9</a> O Israel, trust thou in the LORD: he is their help and their shield. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:10">115:10</a> O house of Aaron, trust in the LORD: he is their help and their shield. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:11">115:11</a> Ye that fear the LORD, trust in the LORD: he is their help and their shield. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:12">115:12</a> The LORD hath been mindful of us: he will bless us; he will bless the house of Israel; he will bless the house of Aaron. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:13">115:13</a> He will bless them that fear the LORD, both small and great. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:14">115:14</a> The LORD will increase you more and more, you and your children. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:15">115:15</a> Ye are blessed of the LORD who made heaven and earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:16">115:16</a> The heaven, even the heavens, are the LORD'S: but the earth hath he given to the children of men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:17">115:17</a> The dead praise not the LORD, neither any that go down into silence. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:18">115:18</a> But we will bless the LORD from this time forth and for ever. Praise the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:1">116:1</a> I love the LORD, because he hath heard my voice and my supplications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:2">116:2</a> Because he hath inclined his ear to me, therefore will I call upon him as long as I live. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:3">116:3</a> The sorrows of death encompassed me, and the pains of hell came upon me: I found trouble and sorrow. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:4">116:4</a> Then I called upon the name of the LORD; O LORD, I beseech thee, deliver my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:5">116:5</a> Gracious is the LORD, and righteous; yes, our God is merciful. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:6">116:6</a> The LORD preserveth the simple: I was brought low, and he helped me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:7">116:7</a> Return to thy rest, O my soul; for the LORD hath dealt bountifully with thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:8">116:8</a> For thou hast delivered my soul from death, my eyes from tears, and my feet from falling. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:9">116:9</a> I will walk before the LORD in the land of the living. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:10">116:10</a> I believed, therefore have I spoken: I was greatly afflicted: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:11">116:11</a> I said in my haste, All men are liars. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:12">116:12</a> What shall I render to the LORD for all his benefits towards me? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:13">116:13</a> I will take the cup of salvation, and call upon the name of the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:14">116:14</a> I will pay my vows to the LORD now in the presence of all his people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:15">116:15</a> Precious in the sight of the LORD is the death of his saints. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:16">116:16</a> O LORD, truly I am thy servant; I am thy servant, the son of thy handmaid: thou hast loosed my bonds. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:17">116:17</a> I will offer to thee the sacrifice of thanksgiving, and will call upon the name of the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:18">116:18</a> I will pay my vows to the LORD now in the presence of all his people, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:19">116:19</a> In the courts of the LORD'S house, in the midst of thee, O Jerusalem. Praise ye the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:1">117:1</a> O praise the LORD, all ye nations: praise him, all ye people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:2">117:2</a> For his merciful kindness is great towards us: and the truth of the LORD endureth for ever. Praise ye the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:1">118:1</a> O give thanks to the LORD; for he is good: because his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:2">118:2</a> Let Israel now say, that his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:3">118:3</a> Let the house of Aaron now say, that his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:4">118:4</a> Let them now that fear the LORD say, that his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:5">118:5</a> I called upon the LORD in distress: the LORD answered me, and set me in a large place. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:6">118:6</a> The LORD is on my side; I will not fear: what can man do to me? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:7">118:7</a> The LORD taketh my part with them that help me: therefore shall I see my desire upon them that hate me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:8">118:8</a> It is better to trust in the LORD than to put confidence in man. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:9">118:9</a> It is better to trust in the LORD than to put confidence in princes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:10">118:10</a> All nations encompassed me: but in the name of the LORD will I destroy them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:11">118:11</a> They encompassed me; yes, they encompassed me: but in the name of the LORD I will destroy them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:12">118:12</a> They encompassed me like bees; they are quenched as the fire of thorns: for in the name of the LORD I will destroy them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:13">118:13</a> Thou hast violently thrust at me that I might fall: but the LORD helped me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:14">118:14</a> The LORD is my strength and song, and is become my salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:15">118:15</a> The voice of rejoicing and salvation is in the tabernacles of the righteous: the right hand of the LORD doeth valiantly. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:16">118:16</a> The right hand of the LORD is exalted: the right hand of the LORD doeth valiantly. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:17">118:17</a> I shall not die, but live, and declare the works of the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:18">118:18</a> The LORD hath chastened me severely: but he hath not given me over to death. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:19">118:19</a> Open to me the gates of righteousness: I will enter them, and I will praise the LORD: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:20">118:20</a> This gate of the LORD, into which the righteous shall enter. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:21">118:21</a> I will praise thee: for thou hast heard me, and art become my salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:22">118:22</a> The stone which the builders refused is become the head stone of the corner. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:23">118:23</a> This is the LORD'S doing; it is wonderful in our eyes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:24">118:24</a> This is the day which the LORD hath made; we will rejoice and be glad in it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:25">118:25</a> Save now, I beseech thee, O LORD: O LORD, I beseech thee, send now prosperity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:26">118:26</a> Blessed be he that cometh in the name of the LORD: we have blessed you out of the house of the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:27">118:27</a> God is the LORD, who hath shown us light: bind the sacrifice with cords, even to the horns of the altar. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:28">118:28</a> Thou art my God, and I will praise thee: thou art my God, I will exalt thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:29">118:29</a> O give thanks to the LORD; for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:1">119:1</a> ALEPH. Blessed are the undefiled in the way, who walk in the law of the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:2">119:2</a> Blessed are they that keep his testimonies, and that seek him with the whole heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:3">119:3</a> They also do no iniquity: they walk in his ways. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:4">119:4</a> Thou hast commanded us to keep thy precepts diligently. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:5">119:5</a> O that my ways were directed to keep thy statutes! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:6">119:6</a> Then shall I not be ashamed, when I have respect to all thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:7">119:7</a> I will praise thee with uprightness of heart, when I shall have learned thy righteous judgments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:8">119:8</a> I will keep thy statutes: O forsake me not utterly. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:9">119:9</a> BETH. Wherewith shall a young man cleanse his way? by taking heed to it, according to thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:10">119:10</a> With my whole heart have I sought thee: O let me not wander from thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:11">119:11</a> Thy word have I hid in my heart, that I might not sin against thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:12">119:12</a> Blessed art thou, O LORD: teach me thy statutes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:13">119:13</a> With my lips have I declared all the judgments of thy mouth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:14">119:14</a> I have rejoiced in the way of thy testimonies, as much as in all riches. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:15">119:15</a> I will meditate in thy precepts, and have respect to thy ways. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:16">119:16</a> I will delight myself in thy statutes: I will not forget thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:17">119:17</a> GIMEL. Deal bountifully with thy servant, that I may live, and keep thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:18">119:18</a> Open thou my eyes, that I may behold wondrous things out of thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:19">119:19</a> I am a stranger in the earth: hide not thy commandments from me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:20">119:20</a> My soul breaketh for the longing that it hath to thy judgments at all times. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:21">119:21</a> Thou hast rebuked the proud that are cursed, who do err from thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:22">119:22</a> Remove from me reproach and contempt; for I have kept thy testimonies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:23">119:23</a> Princes also did sit and speak against me: but thy servant did meditate in thy statutes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:24">119:24</a> Thy testimonies also are my delight, and my counselors. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:25">119:25</a> DALETH. My soul cleaveth to the dust: revive thou me according to thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:26">119:26</a> I have declared my ways, and thou heardest me: teach me thy statutes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:27">119:27</a> Make me to understand the way of thy precepts: so shall I talk of thy wondrous works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:28">119:28</a> My soul melteth for heaviness: strengthen thou me according to thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:29">119:29</a> Remove from me the way of lying: and grant me thy law graciously. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:30">119:30</a> I have chosen the way of truth: thy judgments have I laid before me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:31">119:31</a> I have adhered to thy testimonies: O LORD, put me not to shame. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:32">119:32</a> I will run the way of thy commandments, when thou shalt enlarge my heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:33">119:33</a> HE. Teach me, O LORD, the way of thy statutes; and I shall keep it to the end. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:34">119:34</a> Give me understanding, and I shall keep thy law; yes, I shall observe it with my whole heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:35">119:35</a> Make me to go in the path of thy commandments; for in that do I delight. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:36">119:36</a> Incline my heart to thy testimonies, and not to covetousness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:37">119:37</a> Turn away my eyes from beholding vanity; and revive thou me in thy way. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:38">119:38</a> Establish thy word to thy servant, who is devoted to thy fear. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:39">119:39</a> Turn away my reproach which I fear: for thy judgments are good. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:40">119:40</a> Behold, I have longed after thy precepts: revive me in thy righteousness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:41">119:41</a> VAU. Let thy mercies come also to me, O LORD, even thy salvation, according to thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:42">119:42</a> So shall I have with which to answer him that reproacheth me: for I trust in thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:43">119:43</a> And take not the word of truth utterly out of my mouth; for I have hoped in thy judgments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:44">119:44</a> So shall I keep thy law continually for ever and ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:45">119:45</a> And I will walk at liberty: for I seek thy precepts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:46">119:46</a> I will speak of thy testimonies also before kings, and will not be ashamed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:47">119:47</a> And I will delight myself in thy commandments, which I have loved. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:48">119:48</a> My hands also will I lift to thy commandments, which I have loved; and I will meditate in thy statutes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:49">119:49</a> ZAIN. Remember the word to thy servant, upon which thou hast caused me to hope. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:50">119:50</a> This is my comfort in my affliction: for thy word hath revived me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:51">119:51</a> The proud have had me greatly in derision: yet I have not declined from thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:52">119:52</a> I remembered thy judgments of old, O LORD; and have comforted myself. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:53">119:53</a> Horror hath taken hold upon me because of the wicked that forsake thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:54">119:54</a> Thy statutes have been my songs in the house of my pilgrimage. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:55">119:55</a> I have remembered thy name, O LORD, in the night, and have kept thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:56">119:56</a> This I had, because I kept thy precepts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:57">119:57</a> CHETH. Thou art my portion, O LORD: I have said that I would keep thy words. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:58">119:58</a> I entreated thy favor with my whole heart: be merciful to me according to thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:59">119:59</a> I thought on my ways, and turned my feet to thy testimonies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:60">119:60</a> I made haste, and delayed not to keep thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:61">119:61</a> The bands of the wicked have robbed me: but I have not forgotten thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:62">119:62</a> At midnight I will rise to give thanks to thee, because of thy righteous judgments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:63">119:63</a> I am a companion of all them that fear thee, and of them that keep thy precepts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:64">119:64</a> The earth, O LORD, is full of thy mercy: teach me thy statutes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:65">119:65</a> TETH. Thou hast dealt well with thy servant, O LORD, according to thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:66">119:66</a> Teach me good judgment and knowledge: for I have believed thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:67">119:67</a> Before I was afflicted I went astray: but now have I kept thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:68">119:68</a> Thou art good, and doest good; teach me thy statutes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:69">119:69</a> The proud have forged a lie against me: but I will keep thy precepts with my whole heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:70">119:70</a> Their heart is as gross as fat; but I delight in thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:71">119:71</a> It is good for me that I have been afflicted; that I might learn thy statutes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:72">119:72</a> The law of thy mouth is better to me than thousands of gold and silver. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:73">119:73</a> JOD. Thy hands have made me and fashioned me: give me understanding, that I may learn thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:74">119:74</a> They that fear thee will be glad when they see me; because I have hoped in thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:75">119:75</a> I know, O LORD, that thy judgments are right, and that thou in faithfulness hast afflicted me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:76">119:76</a> Let, I pray thee, thy merciful kindness be for my comfort, according to thy word to thy servant. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:77">119:77</a> Let thy tender mercies come to me, that I may live: for thy law is my delight. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:78">119:78</a> Let the proud be ashamed; for they dealt perversely with me without a cause: but I will meditate in thy precepts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:79">119:79</a> Let those that fear thee turn to me, and those that have known thy testimonies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:80">119:80</a> Let my heart be sound in thy statutes; that I may not be ashamed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:81">119:81</a> CAPH. My soul fainteth for thy salvation: but I hope in thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:82">119:82</a> My eyes fail for thy word, saying, When wilt thou comfort me? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:83">119:83</a> For I am become like a bottle in the smoke; yet I do not forget thy statutes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:84">119:84</a> How many are the days of thy servant? when wilt thou execute judgment on them that persecute me? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:85">119:85</a> The proud have digged pits for me, which are not according to thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:86">119:86</a> All thy commandments are faithful: they persecute me wrongfully; help thou me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:87">119:87</a> They had almost consumed me upon earth; but I forsook not thy precepts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:88">119:88</a> Revive me after thy loving-kindness; so shall I keep the testimony of thy mouth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:89">119:89</a> LAMED. For ever, O LORD, thy word is settled in heaven. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:90">119:90</a> Thy faithfulness is to all generations: thou hast established the earth, and it abideth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:91">119:91</a> They continue this day according to thy ordinances: for all are thy servants. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:92">119:92</a> Unless thy law had been my delights, I should then have perished in my affliction. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:93">119:93</a> I will never forget thy precepts: for with them thou hast revived me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:94">119:94</a> I am thine, save me; for I have sought thy precepts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:95">119:95</a> The wicked have waited for me to destroy me: but I will consider thy testimonies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:96">119:96</a> I have seen an end of all perfection: but thy commandment is exceeding broad. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:97">119:97</a> MEM. O how I love thy law! it is my meditation all the day. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:98">119:98</a> Thou through thy commandments hast made me wiser than my enemies: for they are ever with me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:99">119:99</a> I have more understanding than all my teachers: for thy testimonies are my meditation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:100">119:100</a> I understand more than the ancients, because I keep thy precepts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:101">119:101</a> I have refrained my feet from every evil way, that I might keep thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:102">119:102</a> I have not departed from thy judgments: for thou hast taught me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:103">119:103</a> How sweet are thy words to my taste! yes, sweeter than honey to my mouth! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:104">119:104</a> Through thy precepts I get understanding: therefore I hate every false way. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:105">119:105</a> NUN. Thy word is a lamp to my feet, and a light to my path. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:106">119:106</a> I have sworn, and I will perform it, that I will keep thy righteous judgments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:107">119:107</a> I am afflicted very much: revive me, O LORD, according to thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:108">119:108</a> Accept, I beseech thee, the free-will-offerings of my mouth, O LORD, and teach me thy judgments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:109">119:109</a> My soul is continually in my hand: yet I do not forget thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:110">119:110</a> The wicked have laid a snare for me: yet I erred not from thy precepts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:111">119:111</a> Thy testimonies have I taken as an heritage for ever: for they are the rejoicing of my heart. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:112">119:112</a> I have inclined my heart to perform thy statutes always, even to the end. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:113">119:113</a> SAMECH. I hate vain thoughts: but thy law do I love. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:114">119:114</a> Thou art my hiding place and my shield: I hope in thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:115">119:115</a> Depart from me, ye evil-doers: for I will keep the commandments of my God. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:116">119:116</a> Uphold me according to thy word, that I may live: and let me not be ashamed of my hope. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:117">119:117</a> Support me, and I shall be safe: and I will have respect to thy statutes continually. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:118">119:118</a> Thou hast trodden down all them that err from thy statutes: for their deceit is falsehood. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:119">119:119</a> Thou puttest away all the wicked of the earth like dross: therefore I love thy testimonies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:120">119:120</a> My flesh trembleth for fear of thee; and I am afraid of thy judgments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:121">119:121</a> AIN. I have done judgment and justice; leave me not to my oppressors. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:122">119:122</a> Be surety for thy servant for good: let not the proud oppress me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:123">119:123</a> My eyes fail for thy salvation, and for the word of thy righteousness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:124">119:124</a> Deal with thy servant according to thy mercy, and teach me thy statutes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:125">119:125</a> I am thy servant; give me understanding, that I may know thy testimonies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:126">119:126</a> It is time for thee, LORD, to work: for they have made void thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:127">119:127</a> Therefore I love thy commandments above gold; yes, above fine gold. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:128">119:128</a> Therefore I esteem all thy precepts concerning all things to be right; and I hate every false way. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:129">119:129</a> PE. Thy testimonies are wonderful: therefore doth my soul keep them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:130">119:130</a> The entrance of thy words giveth light; it giveth understanding to the simple. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:131">119:131</a> I opened my mouth, and panted: for I longed for thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:132">119:132</a> Look thou upon me, and be merciful to me, as thou usest to do to those that love thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:133">119:133</a> Order my steps in thy word: and let not any iniquity have dominion over me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:134">119:134</a> Deliver me from the oppression of man: so will I keep thy precepts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:135">119:135</a> Make thy face to shine upon thy servant: and teach me thy statutes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:136">119:136</a> Rivers of waters run down my eyes, because they keep not thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:137">119:137</a> TSADDI. Righteous art thou, O LORD, and upright are thy judgments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:138">119:138</a> Thy testimonies that thou hast commanded are righteous and very faithful. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:139">119:139</a> My zeal hath consumed me; because my enemies have forgotten thy words. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:140">119:140</a> Thy word is very pure: therefore thy servant loveth it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:141">119:141</a> I am small and despised: yet I do not forget thy precepts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:142">119:142</a> Thy righteousness is an everlasting righteousness, and thy law is the truth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:143">119:143</a> Trouble and anguish have taken hold on me: yet thy commandments are my delights. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:144">119:144</a> The righteousness of thy testimonies is everlasting: give me understanding, and I shall live. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:145">119:145</a> KOPH. I cried with my whole heart; hear me, O LORD: I will keep thy statutes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:146">119:146</a> I cried to thee; save me, and I shall keep thy testimonies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:147">119:147</a> I came before the dawning of the morning, and cried: I hoped in thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:148">119:148</a> My eyes anticipated the night watches, that I might meditate in thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:149">119:149</a> Hear my voice, according to thy loving-kindness: O LORD, revive me according to thy judgment. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:150">119:150</a> They draw nigh that follow after mischief: they are far from thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:151">119:151</a> Thou art near, O LORD; and all thy commandments are truth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:152">119:152</a> Concerning thy testimonies, I have known of old that thou hast founded them for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:153">119:153</a> RESH. Consider my affliction, and deliver me: for I do not forget thy law. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:154">119:154</a> Plead my cause, and deliver me: revive me according to thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:155">119:155</a> Salvation is far from the wicked: for they seek not thy statutes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:156">119:156</a> Great are thy tender mercies, O LORD: revive me according to thy judgments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:157">119:157</a> Many are my persecutors and my enemies; yet I do not decline from thy testimonies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:158">119:158</a> I beheld the transgressors, and was grieved; because they kept not thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:159">119:159</a> Consider how I love thy precepts: revive me, O LORD, according to thy loving-kindness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:160">119:160</a> Thy word is true from the beginning: and every one of thy righteous judgments endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:161">119:161</a> SCHIN. Princes have persecuted me without a cause; but my heart standeth in awe of thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:162">119:162</a> I rejoice at thy word, as one that findeth great spoil. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:163">119:163</a> I hate and abhor lying: but thy law do I love. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:164">119:164</a> Seven times a day do I praise thee, because of thy righteous judgments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:165">119:165</a> Great peace have they who love thy law: and nothing shall cause them to stumble. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:166">119:166</a> LORD, I have hoped for thy salvation, and performed thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:167">119:167</a> My soul hath kept thy testimonies; and I love them exceedingly. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:168">119:168</a> I have kept thy precepts and thy testimonies: for all my ways are before thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:169">119:169</a> TAU. Let my cry come near before thee, O LORD: give me understanding according to thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:170">119:170</a> Let my supplication come before thee: deliver me according to thy word. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:171">119:171</a> My lips shall utter praise, when thou hast taught me thy statutes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:172">119:172</a> My tongue shall speak of thy word: for all thy commandments are righteousness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:173">119:173</a> Let thy hand help me; for I have chosen thy precepts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:174">119:174</a> I have longed for thy salvation, O LORD; and thy law is my delight. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:175">119:175</a> Let my soul live, and it shall praise thee; and let thy judgments help me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:176">119:176</a> I have gone astray like a lost sheep; seek thy servant; for I do not forget thy commandments. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:1">120:1</a> A Song of degrees. In my distress I cried to the LORD, and he heard me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:2">120:2</a> Deliver my soul, O LORD, from lying lips, and from a deceitful tongue. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:3">120:3</a> What shall be given to thee? or what shall be done to thee, thou false tongue? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:4">120:4</a> Sharp arrows of the mighty, with coals of juniper. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:5">120:5</a> Woe is me, that I sojourn in Mesech, that I dwell in the tents of Kedar! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:6">120:6</a> My soul hath long dwelt with him that hateth peace. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:7">120:7</a> I am for peace: but when I speak, they are for war. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:1">121:1</a> A Song of degrees. I will lift up my eyes to the hills, from whence cometh my help. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:2">121:2</a> My help cometh from the LORD, who made heaven and earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:3">121:3</a> He will not suffer thy foot to be moved: he that keepeth thee will not slumber. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:4">121:4</a> Behold, he that keepeth Israel shall neither slumber nor sleep. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:5">121:5</a> The LORD is thy keeper: the LORD is thy shade upon thy right hand. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:6">121:6</a> The sun shall not smite thee by day, nor the moon by night. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:7">121:7</a> The LORD will preserve thee from all evil: he will preserve thy soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:8">121:8</a> The LORD will preserve thy going out and thy coming in from this time forth, and even for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:1">122:1</a> A Song of degrees of David. I was glad when they said to me, Let us go into the house of the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:2">122:2</a> Our feet shall stand within thy gates, O Jerusalem. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:3">122:3</a> Jerusalem is built as a city that is compact together: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:4">122:4</a> Whither the tribes go up, the tribes of the LORD, to the testimony of Israel, to give thanks to the name of the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:5">122:5</a> For there are set thrones of judgment, the thrones of the house of David. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:6">122:6</a> Pray for the peace of Jerusalem: they shall prosper that love thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:7">122:7</a> Peace be within thy walls, and prosperity within thy palaces. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:8">122:8</a> For my brethren and companions' sake, I will now say, Peace be within thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:9">122:9</a> Because of the house of the LORD our God I will seek thy good. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:1">123:1</a> A Song of degrees. To thee I raise my eyes, O thou that dwellest in the heavens. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:2">123:2</a> Behold, as the eyes of servants look to the hand of their masters, and as the eyes of a maiden to the hand of her mistress; so our eyes wait upon the LORD our God, until he shall have mercy upon us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:3">123:3</a> Have mercy upon us, O LORD, have mercy upon us; for we are exceedingly filled with contempt. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:4">123:4</a> Our soul is exceedingly filled with the scorning of those that are at ease, and with the contempt of the proud. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:1">124:1</a> A Song of degrees of David. If it had not been the LORD who was on our side, now may Israel say; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:2">124:2</a> If it had not been the LORD who was on our side, when men rose up against us: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:3">124:3</a> Then they had swallowed us up quick, when their wrath was kindled against us: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:4">124:4</a> Then the waters had overwhelmed us, the stream had gone over our soul: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:5">124:5</a> Then the proud waters had gone over our soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:6">124:6</a> Blessed be the LORD, who hath not given us as a prey to their teeth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:7">124:7</a> Our soul hath escaped as a bird out of the snare of the fowlers: the snare is broken, and we have escaped. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:8">124:8</a> Our help is in the name of the LORD, who made heaven and earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:1">125:1</a> A Song of degrees. They that trust in the LORD, shall be as mount Zion, which cannot be removed, but abideth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:2">125:2</a> As the mountains are round Jerusalem, so the LORD is around his people from henceforth even for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:3">125:3</a> For the rod of the wicked shall not rest upon the lot of the righteous; lest the righteous put forth their hands to iniquity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:4">125:4</a> Do good, O LORD, to those that are good, and to them that are upright in their hearts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:5">125:5</a> As for such as turn aside to their crooked ways, the LORD shall lead them forth with the workers of iniquity: but peace shall be upon Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:1">126:1</a> A Song of degrees. When the LORD turned again the captivity of Zion, we were like them that dream. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:2">126:2</a> Then was our mouth filled with laughter, and our tongue with singing: then said they among the heathen, The LORD hath done great things for them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:3">126:3</a> The LORD hath done great things for us; of which we are glad. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:4">126:4</a> Turn again our captivity, O LORD, as the streams in the south. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:5">126:5</a> They that sow in tears shall reap in joy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:6">126:6</a> He that goeth forth and weepeth, bearing precious seed, shall doubtless return with rejoicing, bringing his sheaves with him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:1">127:1</a> A Song of degrees for Solomon. Except the LORD shall build the house, they labor in vain that build it: except the LORD shall keep the city, the watchman waketh in vain. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:2">127:2</a> It is vain for you to rise early, to sit up late, to eat the bread of sorrows: for so he giveth his beloved sleep. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:3">127:3</a> Lo, children are a heritage of the LORD: and the fruit of the womb is his reward. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:4">127:4</a> As arrows are in the hand of a mighty man: so are children of the youth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:5">127:5</a> Happy is the man that hath his quiver full of them: they shall not be ashamed, but they shall speak with the enemies in the gate. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:1">128:1</a> A Song of degrees. Blessed is every one that feareth the LORD; that walketh in his ways. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:2">128:2</a> For thou shalt eat the labor of thy hands: happy shalt thou be, and it shall be well with thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:3">128:3</a> Thy wife shall be as a fruitful vine by the sides of thy house: thy children like olive plants around thy table. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:4">128:4</a> Behold, that thus shall the man be blessed that feareth the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:5">128:5</a> The LORD shall bless thee out of Zion: and thou shalt see the good of Jerusalem all the days of thy life. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:6">128:6</a> Yes, thou shalt see thy children's children, and peace upon Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:1">129:1</a> A Song of degrees. Many a time have they afflicted me from my youth, may Israel now say: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:2">129:2</a> Many a time have they afflicted me from my youth: yet they have not prevailed against me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:3">129:3</a> The plowers plowed upon my back: they made long their furrows. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:4">129:4</a> The LORD is righteous: he hath cut asunder the cords of the wicked. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:5">129:5</a> Let them all be confounded and turned back that hate Zion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:6">129:6</a> Let them be as the grass upon the house-tops, which withereth before it groweth up: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:7">129:7</a> With which the mower filleth not his hand; nor he that bindeth sheaves, his bosom. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:8">129:8</a> Neither do they who go by, say, The blessing of the LORD be upon you: we bless you in the name of the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:1">130:1</a> A Song of degrees. Out of the depths have I cried to thee, O LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:2">130:2</a> Lord, hear my voice: let thy ears be attentive to the voice of my supplications. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:3">130:3</a> If thou, LORD, shouldest mark iniquities, O Lord, who shall stand? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:4">130:4</a> But there is forgiveness with thee, that thou mayest be feared. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:5">130:5</a> I wait for the LORD, my soul doth wait, and in his word do I hope. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:6">130:6</a> My soul waiteth for the Lord more than they that watch for the morning: I say, more than they that watch for the morning. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:7">130:7</a> Let Israel hope in the LORD: for with the LORD there is mercy, and with him is plenteous redemption. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:8">130:8</a> And he shall redeem Israel from all his iniquities. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:1">131:1</a> A Song of degrees of David. LORD, my heart is not haughty, nor my eyes lofty: neither do I exercise myself in great matters, or in things too high for me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:2">131:2</a> Surely I have behaved and quieted myself as a child that is weaned by his mother: my soul is even as a weaned child. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:3">131:3</a> Let Israel hope in the LORD from henceforth and for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:1">132:1</a> A Song of degrees. LORD, remember David and all his afflictions; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:2">132:2</a> How he swore to the LORD, and vowed to the mighty God of Jacob; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:3">132:3</a> Surely I will not come into the tabernacle of my house, nor go up into my bed; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:4">132:4</a> I will not give sleep to my eyes, or slumber to my eyelids, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:5">132:5</a> Until I find a place for the LORD, a habitation for the mighty God of Jacob. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:6">132:6</a> Lo, we heard of it at Ephratah: we found it in the fields of the wood. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:7">132:7</a> We will go into his tabernacles: we will worship at his footstool. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:8">132:8</a> Arise, O LORD, into thy rest; thou, and the ark of thy strength. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:9">132:9</a> Let thy priests be clothed with righteousness; and let thy saints shout for joy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:10">132:10</a> For thy servant David's sake turn not away the face of thy anointed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:11">132:11</a> The LORD hath sworn in truth to David; he will not turn from it; Of the fruit of thy body will I set upon thy throne. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:12">132:12</a> If thy children will keep my covenant and my testimony that I shall teach them; their children also shall sit upon thy throne for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:13">132:13</a> For the LORD hath chosen Zion; he hath desired it for his habitation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:14">132:14</a> This is my rest for ever: here will I dwell; for I have desired it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:15">132:15</a> I will abundantly bless her provision: I will satisfy her poor with bread. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:16">132:16</a> I will also clothe her priests with salvation, and her saints shall shout aloud for joy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:17">132:17</a> There will I make the horn of David to bud, I have ordained a lamp for my anointed. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:18">132:18</a> His enemies will I clothe with shame: but upon himself shall his crown flourish. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:1">133:1</a> A Song of degrees of David. Behold, how good and how pleasant it is for brethren to dwell together in unity! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:2">133:2</a> It is like the precious ointment upon the head, that ran down upon the beard, even Aaron's beard: that went down to the skirts of his garment; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:3">133:3</a> As the dew of Hermon, and as the dew that descended upon the mountains of Zion: for there the LORD commanded the blessing, even life for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:1">134:1</a> A Song of degrees. Behold, bless ye the LORD, all ye servants of the LORD, who by night stand in the house of the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:2">134:2</a> Lift up your hands in the sanctuary, and bless the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:3">134:3</a> The LORD that made heaven and earth bless thee out of Zion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:1">135:1</a> Praise ye the LORD. Praise ye the name of the LORD; praise him, O ye servants of the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:2">135:2</a> Ye that stand in the house of the LORD, in the courts of the house of our God, </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:3">135:3</a> Praise the LORD; for the LORD is good; sing praises to his name; for it is pleasant. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:4">135:4</a> For the LORD hath chosen Jacob to himself, and Israel for his peculiar treasure. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:5">135:5</a> For I know that the LORD is great, and that our Lord is above all gods. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:6">135:6</a> Whatever the LORD pleased, that did he in heaven, and in earth, in the seas, and all deep places. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:7">135:7</a> He causeth the vapors to ascend from the ends of the earth; he maketh lightnings for the rain; he bringeth the wind out of his treasuries. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:8">135:8</a> Who smote the first-born of Egypt, both of man and beast. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:9">135:9</a> Who sent tokens and wonders into the midst of thee, O Egypt, upon Pharaoh, and upon all his servants. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:10">135:10</a> Who smote great nations, and slew mighty kings; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:11">135:11</a> Sihon king of the Amorites, and Og king of Bashan, and all the kingdoms of Canaan: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:12">135:12</a> And gave their land for a heritage, a heritage to Israel his people. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:13">135:13</a> Thy name, O LORD, endureth for ever; and thy memorial, O LORD, throughout all generations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:14">135:14</a> For the LORD will judge his people, and he will repent concerning his servants. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:15">135:15</a> The idols of the heathen are silver and gold, the work of men's hands. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:16">135:16</a> They have mouths, but they speak not; eyes have they, but they see not. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:17">135:17</a> They have ears, but they hear not; neither is there any breath in their mouths. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:18">135:18</a> They that make them are like them: so is every one that trusteth in them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:19">135:19</a> Bless the LORD, O house of Israel: bless the LORD, O house of Aaron: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:20">135:20</a> Bless the LORD, O house of Levi: ye that fear the LORD, bless the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:21">135:21</a> Blessed be the LORD out of Zion, who dwelleth at Jerusalem. Praise ye the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:1">136:1</a> O give thanks to the LORD; for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:2">136:2</a> O give thanks to the God of gods: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:3">136:3</a> O give thanks to the Lord of lords: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:4">136:4</a> To him who alone doeth great wonders: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:5">136:5</a> To him that by wisdom made the heavens: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:6">136:6</a> To him that stretched out the earth above the waters: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:7">136:7</a> To him that made great lights: for his mercy endureth for ever: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:8">136:8</a> The sun to rule by day: for his mercy endureth for ever: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:9">136:9</a> The moon and stars to rule by night: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:10">136:10</a> To him that smote Egypt in their first-born: for his mercy endureth for ever: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:11">136:11</a> And brought out Israel from among them: for his mercy endureth for ever: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:12">136:12</a> With a strong hand, and with an out-stretched arm: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:13">136:13</a> To him who divided the Red sea into parts: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:14">136:14</a> And made Israel to pass through the midst of it: for his mercy endureth for ever: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:15">136:15</a> But overthrew Pharaoh and his army in the Red sea: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:16">136:16</a> To him who led his people through the wilderness: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:17">136:17</a> To him who smote great kings: for his mercy endureth for ever: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:18">136:18</a> And slew famous kings: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:19">136:19</a> Sihon king of the Amorites: for his mercy endureth for ever: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:20">136:20</a> And Og king of Bashan: for his mercy endureth for ever: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:21">136:21</a> And gave their land for a heritage: for his mercy endureth for ever: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:22">136:22</a> Even a heritage to Israel his servant: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:23">136:23</a> Who remembered us in our low estate: for his mercy endureth for ever: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:24">136:24</a> And hath redeemed us from our enemies: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:25">136:25</a> Who giveth food to all flesh: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:26">136:26</a> O give thanks to the God of heaven: for his mercy endureth for ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:1">137:1</a> By the rivers of Babylon, there we sat down, yes, we wept, when we remembered Zion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:2">137:2</a> We hung our harps upon the willows in the midst of it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:3">137:3</a> For there they that carried us away captive required of us a song; and they that wasted us required of us mirth, saying, Sing us one of the songs of Zion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:4">137:4</a> How shall we sing the LORD'S song in a foreign land? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:5">137:5</a> If I forget thee, O Jerusalem, let my right hand forget her skill. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:6">137:6</a> If I do not remember thee, let my tongue cleave to the roof of my mouth; if I prefer not Jerusalem above my chief joy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:7">137:7</a> Remember, O LORD, the children of Edom in the day of Jerusalem; who said, Raze it, raze it, even to its foundation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:8">137:8</a> O daughter of Babylon, who art to be destroyed; happy shall he be, that rewardeth thee as thou hast served us. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:9">137:9</a> Happy shall he be, that taketh and dasheth thy little ones against the stones. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:1">138:1</a> A Psalm of David. I will praise thee with my whole heart: before the gods will I sing praise to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:2">138:2</a> I will worship towards thy holy temple, and praise thy name for thy loving-kindness and for thy truth: for thou hast magnified thy word above all thy name. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:3">138:3</a> In the day when I cried thou didst answer me, and strengthen me with strength in my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:4">138:4</a> All the kings of the earth shall praise thee, O LORD, when they hear the words of thy mouth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:5">138:5</a> Yes, they shall sing in the ways of the LORD: for great is the glory of the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:6">138:6</a> Though the LORD is high, yet hath he respect to the lowly: but the proud he knoweth afar off. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:7">138:7</a> Though I walk in the midst of trouble, thou wilt revive me: thou wilt stretch forth thy hand against the wrath of my enemies, and thy right hand will save me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:8">138:8</a> The LORD will perfect that which concerneth me: thy mercy, O LORD, endureth for ever: forsake not the works thy own hands. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:1">139:1</a> To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David. O LORD, thou hast searched me, and known me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:2">139:2</a> Thou knowest my down-sitting and my up rising, thou understandest my thought afar off. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:3">139:3</a> Thou compassest my path and my lying down, and art acquainted with all my ways. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:4">139:4</a> For there is not a word on my tongue, but lo, O LORD, thou knowest it altogether. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:5">139:5</a> Thou hast beset me behind and before, and laid thy hand upon me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:6">139:6</a> Such knowledge is too wonderful for me; it is high, I cannot attain to it. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:7">139:7</a> Whither shall I go from thy spirit? or whither shall I flee from thy presence? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:8">139:8</a> If I ascend into heaven, thou art there: if I make my bed in hell, behold, thou art there. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:9">139:9</a> If I take the wings of the morning, and dwell in the uttermost parts of the sea; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:10">139:10</a> Even there shall thy hand lead me, and thy right hand shall hold me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:11">139:11</a> If I say, Surely the darkness shall cover me; even the night shall be light about me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:12">139:12</a> Yes, the darkness hideth not from thee; but the night shineth as the day: the darkness and the light are both alike to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:13">139:13</a> For thou hast possessed my reins: thou hast covered me in my mother's womb. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:14">139:14</a> I will praise thee: for I am fearfully and wonderfully made: wonderful are thy works; and that my soul well knoweth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:15">139:15</a> My substance was not hid from thee when I was made in secret, and curiously formed in the lowest parts of the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:16">139:16</a> Thy eyes saw my substance, yet being imperfect; and in thy book all my members were written, which in continuance were fashioned, when as yet there was none of them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:17">139:17</a> How precious also are thy thoughts to me, O God! how great is the sum of them! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:18">139:18</a> If I should count them, they are more in number than the sand: when I awake, I am still with thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:19">139:19</a> Surely thou wilt slay the wicked, O God: depart from me therefore, ye bloody men. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:20">139:20</a> For they speak against thee wickedly, and thy enemies take thy name in vain. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:21">139:21</a> Do not I hate them, O LORD, that hate thee? and am not I grieved with those that rise up against thee? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:22">139:22</a> I hate them with perfect hatred: I count them my enemies. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:23">139:23</a> Search me, O God, and know my heart; try me, and know my thoughts: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:24">139:24</a> And see if there is any wicked way in me, and lead me in the way everlasting. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:1">140:1</a> To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David. Deliver me, O LORD, from the evil man: preserve me from the violent man; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:2">140:2</a> Who imagine mischiefs in their heart; continually are they assembled for war. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:3">140:3</a> They have sharpened their tongues like a serpent; adder's poison is under their lips. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:4">140:4</a> Keep me, O LORD, from the hands of the wicked; preserve me from the violent man; who have purposed to overthrow my goings. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:5">140:5</a> The proud have hid a snare for me, and cords; they have spread a net by the way side: they have set gins for me. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:6">140:6</a> I said to the LORD, Thou art my God: hear the voice of my supplications, O LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:7">140:7</a> O GOD the Lord, the strength of my salvation, thou hast covered my head in the day of battle. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:8">140:8</a> Grant not, O LORD, the desires of the wicked: further not his wicked device; lest they exalt themselves. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:9">140:9</a> As for the head of those that encompass me, let the mischief of their own lips cover them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:10">140:10</a> Let burning coals fall upon them: let them be cast into the fire; into deep pits, that they rise not again. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:11">140:11</a> Let not an evil speaker be established on the earth: evil shall hunt the violent man to overthrow him. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:12">140:12</a> I know that the LORD will maintain the cause of the afflicted, and the right of the poor. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:13">140:13</a> Surely the righteous shall give thanks to thy name: the upright shall dwell in thy presence. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:1">141:1</a> A Psalm of David. LORD, I cry to thee: make haste to me; give ear to my voice, when I cry to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:2">141:2</a> Let my prayer be set forth before thee as incense; and the lifting up of my hands as the evening sacrifice. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:3">141:3</a> Set a watch, O LORD, before my mouth; keep the door of my lips. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:4">141:4</a> Incline not my heart to any evil thing, to practice wicked works with men that work iniquity: and let me not eat of their dainties. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:5">141:5</a> Let the righteous smite me; it shall be a kindness: and let him reprove me; it shall be an excellent oil, which shall not break my head: for yet my prayer also shall be in their calamities. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:6">141:6</a> When their judges are overthrown in stony places, they shall hear my words; for they are sweet. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:7">141:7</a> Our bones are scattered at the grave's mouth, as when one cutteth and cleaveth wood upon the earth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:8">141:8</a> But my eyes are to thee, O GOD the Lord: in thee is my trust; leave not my soul destitute. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:9">141:9</a> Keep me from the snare which they have laid for me, and the gins of the workers of iniquity. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:10">141:10</a> Let the wicked fall into their own nets, whilst I escape. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:1">142:1</a> Maschil of David; a prayer when he was in the cave. I cried to the LORD with my voice; with my voice to the LORD I made my supplication. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:2">142:2</a> I poured out my complaint before him; I showed before him my trouble. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:3">142:3</a> When my spirit was overwhelmed within me, then thou knewest my path. In the way in which I walked have they privily laid a snare for me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:4">142:4</a> I looked on my right hand, and beheld, but there was no man that would know me: refuge failed me; no man cared for my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:5">142:5</a> I cried to thee, O LORD: I said, Thou art my refuge and my portion in the land of the living. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:6">142:6</a> Attend to my cry; for I am brought very low: deliver me from my persecutors; for they are stronger than I. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:7">142:7</a> Bring my soul out of prison, that I may praise thy name: the righteous shall encompass me; for thou wilt deal bountifully with me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:1">143:1</a> A Psalm of David. Hear my prayer, O LORD, give ear to my supplications: in thy faithfulness answer me, and in thy righteousness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:2">143:2</a> And enter not into judgment with thy servant: for in thy sight shall no man living be justified. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:3">143:3</a> For the enemy hath persecuted my soul; he hath smitten my life down to the ground; he hath made me to dwell in darkness, as those that have been long dead. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:4">143:4</a> Therefore is my spirit overwhelmed within me; my heart within me is desolate. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:5">143:5</a> I remember the days of old, I meditate on all thy works; I muse on the work of thy hands. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:6">143:6</a> I stretch forth my hands to thee: my soul thirsteth after thee, as a thirsty land. Selah. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:7">143:7</a> Hear me speedily, O LORD: my spirit faileth: hide not thy face from me, lest I be like them that go down into the pit. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:8">143:8</a> Cause me to hear thy loving-kindness in the morning; for in thee do I trust: cause me to know the way in which I should walk; for I lift up my soul to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:9">143:9</a> Deliver me, O LORD, from my enemies: I flee to thee to hide me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:10">143:10</a> Teach me to do thy will; for thou art my God: thy spirit is good; lead me into the land of uprightness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:11">143:11</a> Revive me, O LORD, for thy name's sake: for thy righteousness' sake bring my soul out of trouble. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:12">143:12</a> And of thy mercy cut off my enemies, and destroy all them that afflict my soul: for I am thy servant. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:1">144:1</a> A Psalm of David. Blessed be the LORD my strength, who teacheth my hands to war, and my fingers to fight; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:2">144:2</a> My goodness, and my fortress; my high tower, and my deliverer; my shield, and he in whom I trust; who subdueth my people under me. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:3">144:3</a> LORD, what is man, that thou takest knowledge of him! or the son of man, that thou makest account of him! </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:4">144:4</a> Man is like to vanity: his days are as a shadow that passeth away. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:5">144:5</a> Bow thy heavens, O LORD, and come down: touch the mountains, and they shall smoke. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:6">144:6</a> Cast forth lightning, and scatter them: shoot thy arrows, and destroy them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:7">144:7</a> Send thy hand from above; rid me, and deliver me out of great waters, from the hand of strange children; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:8">144:8</a> Whose mouth speaketh vanity, and their right hand is a right hand of falsehood. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:9">144:9</a> I will sing a new song to thee, O God: upon a psaltery and an instrument of ten strings will I sing praises to thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:10">144:10</a> It is he that giveth salvation to kings: who delivereth David his servant from the hurtful sword. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:11">144:11</a> Rid me, and deliver me from the hand of strange children, whose mouth speaketh vanity, and their right hand is a right hand of falsehood: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:12">144:12</a> That our sons may be as plants grown up in their youth; that our daughters may be as corner stones, polished after the similitude of a palace: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:13">144:13</a> That our granaries may be full, affording all manner of store; that our sheep may bring forth thousands and ten thousands in our streets: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:14">144:14</a> That our oxen may be strong to labor; that there be no breaking in, nor going out; that there be no complaining in our streets. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:15">144:15</a> Happy is that people, that is in such a case: yes, happy is that people, whose God is the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:1">145:1</a> David's Psalm of praise. I will extol thee, my God, O king; and I will bless thy name for ever and ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:2">145:2</a> Every day will I bless thee; and I will praise thy name for ever and ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:3">145:3</a> Great is the LORD, and greatly to be praised; and his greatness is unsearchable. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:4">145:4</a> One generation shall praise thy works to another, and shall declare thy mighty acts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:5">145:5</a> I will speak of the glorious honor of thy majesty, and of thy wondrous works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:6">145:6</a> And men shall speak of the might of thy terrible acts: and I will declare thy greatness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:7">145:7</a> They shall abundantly utter the memory of thy great goodness, and shall sing of thy righteousness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:8">145:8</a> The LORD is gracious, and full of compassion; slow to anger, and of great mercy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:9">145:9</a> The LORD is good to all: and his tender mercies are over all his works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:10">145:10</a> All thy works shall praise thee, O LORD; and thy saints shall bless thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:11">145:11</a> They shall speak of the glory of thy kingdom, and talk of thy power; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:12">145:12</a> To make known to the sons of men his mighty acts, and the glorious majesty of his kingdom. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:13">145:13</a> Thy kingdom is an everlasting kingdom, and thy dominion endureth throughout all generations. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:14">145:14</a> The LORD upholdeth all that fall, and raiseth up all those that are bowed down. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:15">145:15</a> The eyes of all wait upon thee; and thou givest them their food in due season. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:16">145:16</a> Thou openest thy hand, and satisfiest the desire of every living creature. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:17">145:17</a> The LORD is righteous in all his ways, and holy in all his works. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:18">145:18</a> The LORD is nigh to all them that call upon him, to all that call upon him in truth. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:19">145:19</a> He will fulfill the desire of them that fear him: he also will hear their cry, and will save them. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:20">145:20</a> The LORD preserveth all them that love him: but all the wicked will he destroy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:21">145:21</a> My mouth shall speak the praise of the LORD: and let all flesh bless his holy name for ever and ever. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:1">146:1</a> Praise ye the LORD. Praise the LORD, O my soul. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:2">146:2</a> While I live will I praise the LORD: I will sing praises to my God while I have any being. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:3">146:3</a> Put not your trust in princes, nor in the son of man, in whom there is no help. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:4">146:4</a> His breath goeth forth, he returneth to his earth; in that very day his thoughts perish. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:5">146:5</a> Happy is he that hath the God of Jacob for his help, whose hope is in the LORD his God: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:6">146:6</a> Who made heaven, and earth, the sea, and all that is in them: who keepeth truth for ever: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:7">146:7</a> Who executeth judgment for the oppressed: who giveth food to the hungry. The LORD looseth the prisoners: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:8">146:8</a> The LORD openeth the eyes of the blind: the LORD raiseth them that are bowed down: the LORD loveth the righteous: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:9">146:9</a> The LORD preserveth the strangers; he relieveth the fatherless and widow: but the way of the wicked he turneth upside down. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:10">146:10</a> The LORD will reign for ever, even thy God, O Zion, to all generations. Praise ye the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:1">147:1</a> Praise ye the LORD: for it is good to sing praises to our God; for it is pleasant; and praise is comely. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:2">147:2</a> The LORD buildeth up Jerusalem: he gathereth together the outcasts of Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:3">147:3</a> He healeth the broken in heart, and bindeth up their wounds. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:4">147:4</a> He telleth the number of the stars; he calleth them all by their names. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:5">147:5</a> Great is our Lord, and of great power: his understanding is infinite. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:6">147:6</a> The LORD lifteth up the meek: he casteth the wicked down to the ground. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:7">147:7</a> Sing to the LORD with thanksgiving; sing praise upon the harp to our God: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:8">147:8</a> Who covereth the heaven with clouds, who prepareth rain for the earth, who maketh grass to grow upon the mountains. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:9">147:9</a> He giveth to the beast his food, and to the young ravens which cry. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:10">147:10</a> He delighteth not in the strength of the horse: he taketh not pleasure in the legs of a man. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:11">147:11</a> The LORD taketh pleasure in them that fear him, in those that hope in his mercy. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:12">147:12</a> Praise the LORD, O Jerusalem; praise thy God, O Zion. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:13">147:13</a> For he hath strengthened the bars of thy gates; he hath blessed thy children within thee. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:14">147:14</a> He maketh peace in thy borders, and filleth thee with the finest of the wheat. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:15">147:15</a> He sendeth forth his commandment upon earth: his word runneth very swiftly. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:16">147:16</a> He giveth snow like wool: he scattereth the hoar-frost like ashes. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:17">147:17</a> He casteth forth his ice like morsels: who can stand before his cold? </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:18">147:18</a> He sendeth out his word, and melteth them: he causeth his wind to blow, and the waters flow. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:19">147:19</a> He showeth his word to Jacob, his statutes and his judgments to Israel. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:20">147:20</a> He hath not dealt so with any nation: and as for his judgments, they have not known them. Praise ye the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:1">148:1</a> Praise ye the LORD. Praise ye the LORD from the heavens: praise him in the hights. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:2">148:2</a> Praise ye him, all his angels: praise ye him, all his hosts. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:3">148:3</a> Praise ye him, sun and moon: praise him, all ye stars of light. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:4">148:4</a> Praise him, ye heavens of heavens, and ye waters that are above the heavens. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:5">148:5</a> Let them praise the name of the LORD: for he commanded, and they were created. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:6">148:6</a> He hath also established them for ever and ever: he hath made a decree which shall not pass. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:7">148:7</a> Praise the LORD from the earth, ye dragons, and all deeps: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:8">148:8</a> Fire, and hail; snow, and vapors; stormy wind fulfilling his word: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:9">148:9</a> Mountains, and all hills; fruitful trees, and all cedars: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:10">148:10</a> Beasts, and all cattle; creeping animals, and flying fowl: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:11">148:11</a> Kings of the earth, and all people; princes, and all judges of the earth: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:12">148:12</a> Both young men, and maidens; old men, and children: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:13">148:13</a> Let them praise the name of the LORD: for his name alone is excellent; his glory is above the earth and heaven. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:14">148:14</a> He also exalteth the horn of his people, the praise of all his saints; even of the children of Israel, a people near to him. Praise ye the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:1">149:1</a> Praise ye the LORD. Sing to the LORD a new song, and his praise in the congregation of saints. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:2">149:2</a> Let Israel rejoice in him that made him: let the children of Zion be joyful in their King. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:3">149:3</a> Let them praise his name in the dance: let them sing praises to him with the timbrel and harp: </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:4">149:4</a> For the LORD taketh pleasure in his people: he will beautify the meek with salvation. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:5">149:5</a> Let the saints be joyful in glory: let them sing aloud upon their beds. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:6">149:6</a> Let the high praises of God be in their mouth, and a two-edged sword in their hand; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:7">149:7</a> To execute vengeance upon the heathen, and punishments upon the people; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:8">149:8</a> To bind their kings with chains, and their nobles with fetters of iron; </p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:9">149:9</a> To execute upon them the judgment written: this honor have all his saints. Praise ye the LORD. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:1">150:1</a> Praise ye the LORD. Praise God in his sanctuary: praise him in the firmament of his power. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:2">150:2</a> Praise him for his mighty acts: praise him according to his excellent greatness. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:3">150:3</a> Praise him with the sound of the trumpet: praise him with the psaltery and harp. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:4">150:4</a> Praise him with the timbrel and dance: praise him with stringed instruments and organs. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:5">150:5</a> Praise him upon the loud cymbals: praise him upon the high sounding cymbals. </p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:6">150:6</a> Let every thing that hath breath praise the LORD. Praise ye the LORD. </p> 
 <p></p><hr>

 </body>
